R-C2: Cycle-Consistent Reinforcement Learning Improves Multimodal Reasoning
Authors: Zirui Zhang, Haoyu Dong, Kexin Pei, Chengzhi Mao
First: 2026-03-26T17:58:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T17:58:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Robust perception and reasoning require consistency across sensory modalities. Yet current multimodal models often violate this principle, yielding contradictory predictions for visual and textual representations of the same concept. Rather than masking these failures with standard voting mechanisms, which can amplify systematic biases, we show that cross-modal inconsistency provides a rich and natural signal for learning. We introduce RC2, a reinforcement learning framework that resolves internal conflicts by enforcing cross-modal cycle consistency. By requiring a model to perform backward inference, switch modalities, and reliably reconstruct the answer through forward inference, we obtain a dense, label-free reward. This cyclic constraint encourages the model to align its internal representations autonomously. Optimizing for this structure mitigates modality-specific errors and improves reasoning accuracy by up to 7.6 points. Our results suggest that advanced reasoning emerges not only from scaling data, but also from enforcing a structurally consistent understanding of the world.
中文标题/摘要
标题：R-C2：循环一致性强化学习提升多模态推理能力
稳健的感知与推理需要跨感官模态的一致性。然而当前多模态模型常违背此原则，对同一概念的视觉与文本表征产生矛盾预测。不同于通过可能放大系统性偏差的标准投票机制掩盖这些缺陷，我们证明跨模态不一致性为学习提供了丰富且自然的信号。我们提出RC2强化学习框架，通过强制跨模态循环一致性来解决内部冲突。该方法要求模型执行反向推理、切换模态，并通过前向推理可靠重构答案，从而获得密集的无标签奖励。这种循环约束促使模型自主对齐其内部表征。优化该结构可缓解模态特异性误差，将推理准确率最高提升7.6个百分点。结果表明，高级推理能力的涌现不仅源于数据规模扩展，更依赖于对世界构建结构一致的理解。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the observation that current multimodal models often produce contradictory predictions across different sensory modalities, which undermines robust perception and reasoning. To address this, the authors introduce RC2, a reinforcement learning framework that enforces cross-modal cycle consistency by requiring models to perform backward inference, switch modalities, and reconstruct answers through forward inference, thereby generating a dense, label-free reward signal. Experimental results show that this approach reduces modality-specific errors and improves reasoning accuracy by up to 7.6 points, suggesting that structural consistency, beyond mere data scaling, is key to advanced reasoning.
本文的动机在于观察到当前多模态模型常在不同感官模态间产生矛盾预测，这削弱了稳健的感知与推理能力。为解决此问题，作者提出了RC2，一个强化学习框架，通过要求模型执行反向推理、切换模态并通过前向推理重建答案来强制跨模态循环一致性，从而生成密集的无标签奖励信号。实验结果表明，该方法减少了模态特定错误，并将推理准确率提升了高达7.6个百分点，表明结构一致性（而非仅数据扩展）对高级推理至关重要。
LanteRn: Latent Visual Structured Reasoning
Authors: André G. Viveiros, Nuno Gonçalves, Matthias Lindemann, André Martins
First: 2026-03-26T16:41:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T16:41:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While language reasoning models excel in many tasks, visual reasoning remains challenging for current large multimodal models (LMMs). As a result, most LMMs default to verbalizing perceptual content into text, a strong limitation for tasks requiring fine-grained spatial and visual understanding. While recent approaches take steps toward thinking with images by invoking tools or generating intermediate images, they either rely on external modules, or incur unnecessary computation by reasoning directly in pixel space. In this paper, we introduce LanteRn, a framework that enables LMMs to interleave language with compact latent visual representations, allowing visual reasoning to occur directly in latent space. LanteRn augments a vision-language transformer with the ability to generate and attend to continuous visual thought embeddings during inference. We train the model in two stages: supervised fine-tuning to ground visual features in latent states, followed by reinforcement learning to align latent reasoning with task-level utility. We evaluate LanteRn on three perception-centric benchmarks (VisCoT, V*, and Blink), observing consistent improvements in visual grounding and fine-grained reasoning. These results suggest that internal latent representations provide a promising direction for more efficient multimodal reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LanteRn：潜在视觉结构化推理
尽管语言推理模型在许多任务中表现出色，但视觉推理对当前大型多模态模型仍具挑战性。因此，大多数多模态模型默认将感知内容转化为文本，这对需要细粒度空间与视觉理解的任务构成严重限制。近期方法虽通过调用工具或生成中间图像向视觉推理迈进，但它们要么依赖外部模块，要么因直接在像素空间推理而产生不必要的计算开销。本文提出LanteRn框架，使多模态模型能够将语言与紧凑的潜在视觉表征交织，实现直接在潜在空间进行视觉推理。LanteRn通过增强视觉语言Transformer，使其在推理过程中能生成并关注连续的视觉思维嵌入。我们采用两阶段训练：首先通过监督微调将视觉特征锚定于潜在状态，再通过强化学习使潜在推理与任务级效用对齐。在三个以感知为核心的基准测试（VisCoT、V*和Blink）中评估LanteRn，观察到其在视觉定位与细粒度推理方面均取得持续改进。这些结果表明，内部潜在表征为更高效的多模态推理提供了可行方向。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for LanteRn stems from the limitations of current large multimodal models in visual reasoning, which often default to converting visual content into text, thereby losing fine-grained spatial and visual understanding. The method introduces a framework that enables these models to interleave language with compact latent visual representations, allowing reasoning to occur directly in latent space by augmenting a vision-language transformer to generate and attend to continuous visual thought embeddings during inference, trained via supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning. Main experimental results show consistent improvements in visual grounding and fine-grained reasoning on perception-centric benchmarks like VisCoT, V*, and Blink, indicating that internal latent representations offer a promising direction for more efficient multimodal reasoning.
LanteRn的动机源于当前大型多模态模型在视觉推理方面的局限性，这些模型通常将视觉内容转换为文本，从而丢失了细粒度的空间和视觉理解。该方法引入了一个框架，使这些模型能够将语言与紧凑的潜在视觉表示交织在一起，通过增强视觉语言Transformer在推理过程中生成和关注连续的视觉思维嵌入，从而在潜在空间中进行直接推理，并通过监督微调和强化学习进行训练。主要实验结果表明，在VisCoT、V*和Blink等感知中心基准测试中，视觉基础和细粒度推理能力得到了一致提升，这表明内部潜在表示为更高效的多模态推理提供了有前景的方向。
Learning When to Act: Interval-Aware Reinforcement Learning with Predictive Temporal Structure
Authors: Davide Di Gioia
First: 2026-03-23T16:46:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T16:30:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autonomous agents operating in continuous environments must decide not only what to do, but when to act. We introduce a lightweight adaptive temporal control system that learns the optimal interval between cognitive ticks from experience, replacing ad hoc biologically inspired timers with a principled learned policy. The policy state is augmented with a predictive hyperbolic spread signal (a "curvature signal" shorthand) derived from hyperbolic geometry: the mean pairwise Poincare distance among n sampled futures embedded in the Poincare ball. High spread indicates a branching, uncertain future and drives the agent to act sooner; low spread signals predictability and permits longer rest intervals. We further propose an interval-aware reward that explicitly penalises inefficiency relative to the chosen wait time, correcting a systematic credit-assignment failure of naive outcome-based rewards in timing problems. We additionally introduce a joint spatio-temporal embedding (ATCPG-ST) that concatenates independently normalised state and position projections in the Poincare ball; spatial trajectory divergence provides an independent timing signal unavailable to the state-only variant (ATCPG-SO). This extension raises mean hyperbolic spread (kappa) from 1.88 to 3.37 and yields a further 5.8 percent efficiency gain over the state-only baseline. Ablation experiments across five random seeds demonstrate that (i) learning is the dominant efficiency factor (54.8 percent over no-learning), (ii) hyperbolic spread provides significant complementary gain (26.2 percent over geometry-free control), (iii) the combined system achieves 22.8 percent efficiency over the fixed-interval baseline, and (iv) adding spatial position information to the spread embedding yields an additional 5.8 percent.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习何时行动：具有预测性时间结构的区间感知强化学习
在连续环境中运行的自主智能体不仅需要决定做什么，还需决定何时行动。本文提出了一种轻量级自适应时间控制系统，该系统通过经验学习认知节拍之间的最优间隔，以基于原则的学习策略替代临时性的生物启发计时器。策略状态通过从双曲几何导出的预测性双曲扩散信号（简称“曲率信号”）进行增强：该信号为嵌入庞加莱球中的n个采样未来之间的平均成对庞加莱距离。高扩散值表示未来分支多、不确定性高，促使智能体更早行动；低扩散值表示可预测性强，允许更长的休息间隔。我们进一步提出一种区间感知奖励，明确惩罚相对于所选等待时间的低效行为，从而修正了在时序问题中基于结果的朴素奖励存在的系统性信用分配缺陷。此外，我们引入了一种联合时空嵌入（ATCPG-ST），将独立归一化的状态和位置投影在庞加莱球中拼接；空间轨迹发散提供了仅状态变体（ATCPG-SO）无法获得的独立时序信号。这一扩展将平均双曲扩散值（kappa）从1.88提升至3.37，并在仅状态基线基础上进一步实现了5.8%的效率增益。基于五个随机种子的消融实验表明：（i）学习是主导效率因素（相比无学习提升54.8%），（ii）双曲扩散提供显著的互补增益（相比无几何控制提升26.2%），（iii）组合系统相比固定间隔基线实现22.8%的效率提升，（iv）在扩散嵌入中添加空间位置信息可额外带来5.8%的增益。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge for autonomous agents in continuous environments to determine optimal action timing, moving beyond fixed or biologically inspired intervals. It introduces a lightweight adaptive temporal control system that learns an optimal action interval policy, augmented with a predictive hyperbolic spread signal derived from the mean pairwise Poincaré distance among sampled future embeddings; this signal quantifies future uncertainty, prompting earlier action when high and permitting longer waits when low. The method also employs an interval-aware reward to correct credit assignment in timing tasks and a joint spatio-temporal embedding (ATCPG-ST) that enhances timing signals. Experimental results across five random seeds show the system achieves a 22.8% efficiency gain over a fixed-interval baseline, with learning contributing 54.8% of the improvement, hyperbolic spread adding 26.2%, and spatial information yielding a further 5.8% gain.
本文针对连续环境中自主智能体需确定最佳行动时机的问题，提出了一种轻量级自适应时间控制系统，以替代固定的或受生物启发的计时器。该方法通过学习最优行动间隔策略，并引入基于双曲几何的预测性扩散信号（即双曲球中采样未来嵌入的平均成对庞加莱距离），该信号量化未来不确定性：高扩散表示分支多、不确定性大，促使智能体提前行动；低扩散则表明可预测性强，允许更长等待间隔。此外，方法采用了间隔感知奖励以修正时序任务中的信用分配问题，并提出了联合时空嵌入（ATCPG-ST）来增强时序信号。在五个随机种子上的消融实验表明，系统相比固定间隔基线实现了22.8%的效率提升，其中学习贡献了54.8%的改进，双曲扩散信号带来26.2%的增益，而添加空间位置信息进一步提高了5.8%。
Cooperative Deep Reinforcement Learning for Fair RIS Allocation
Authors: Martin Mark Zan, Stefan Schwarz
First: 2026-03-26T15:46:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T15:46:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The deployment of reconfigurable intelligent surfaces (RISs) introduces new challenges for resource allocation in multi-cell wireless networks, particularly when user loads are uneven across base stations. In this work, we consider RISs as shared infrastructure that must be dynamically assigned among competing base stations, and we address this problem using a simultaneous ascending auction mechanism. To mitigate performance imbalances between cells, we propose a fairness-aware collaborative multi-agent reinforcement learning approach in which base stations adapt their bidding strategies based on both expected utility gains and relative service quality. A centrally computed performance-dependent fairness indicator is incorporated into the agents' observations, enabling implicit coordination without direct inter-base-station communication. Simulation results show that the proposed framework effectively redistributes RIS resources toward weaker-performing cells, substantially improving the rates of the worst-served users while preserving overall throughput. The results demonstrate that fairness-oriented RIS allocation can be achieved through cooperative learning, providing a flexible tool for balancing efficiency and equity in future wireless networks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于协作深度强化学习的公平可重构智能表面分配
可重构智能表面（RIS）的部署为多小区无线网络的资源分配带来了新的挑战，尤其在基站间用户负载不均衡的情况下。本研究将RIS视为共享基础设施，需在竞争基站间动态分配，并采用同步递增拍卖机制解决该问题。为缓解小区间性能失衡，我们提出一种公平感知的协作多智能体强化学习方法，基站根据预期效用增益和相对服务质量调整其竞价策略。通过将中央计算的性能相关公平指标纳入智能体观测，实现了无需基站间直接通信的隐式协调。仿真结果表明，该框架能有效将RIS资源重新分配给性能较弱的小区，在保持整体吞吐量的同时显著提升服务最差用户的速率。结果证明，通过协作学习可实现面向公平的RIS分配，为未来无线网络中效率与公平的平衡提供了灵活工具。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of fairly allocating reconfigurable intelligent surfaces (RISs) as shared resources in multi-cell wireless networks, where uneven user loads can create performance imbalances between base stations. The authors propose a cooperative multi-agent deep reinforcement learning approach integrated with a simultaneous ascending auction mechanism, enabling base stations to adapt their bidding strategies based on both utility gains and a centrally computed fairness indicator that reflects relative service quality. Experimental simulations demonstrate that this method effectively reallocates RIS resources toward underperforming cells, significantly improving the data rates of the worst-served users while maintaining overall network throughput, thus balancing efficiency and fairness.
本文针对多小区无线网络中可重构智能表面（RIS）作为共享资源分配不公的挑战，特别是在用户负载不均导致基站间性能失衡的场景下，提出了一种解决方案。作者采用协同多智能体深度强化学习方法，结合同步递增拍卖机制，使基站能够根据预期效用增益和中央计算的、反映相对服务质量的公平性指标来调整其竞价策略。仿真结果表明，该方法能有效将RIS资源重新分配给性能较弱的基站，显著提升服务最差用户的速率，同时保持整体网络吞吐量，从而实现了效率与公平性的平衡。
An Integrative Genome-Scale Metabolic Modeling and Machine Learning Framework for Predicting and Optimizing Biofuel-Relevant Biomass Production in Saccharomyces cerevisiae
Authors: Neha K. Nair, Aaron D'Souza
First: 2026-03-26T15:32:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T15:32:16+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 12 figures, and 2 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Saccharomyces cerevisiae is a cornerstone organism in industrial biotechnology, valued for its genetic tractability and robust fermentative capacity. Accurately predicting biomass flux across diverse environmental and genetic perturbations remains a significant challenge for rational strain design. We present a computational framework combining the Yeast9 genome-scale metabolic model with machine learning and optimization to predict, interpret, and enhance biomass flux. Flux balance analysis generated 2,000 flux profiles by varying glucose, oxygen, and ammonium uptake rates. Random Forest and XGBoost regressors achieved R2 of 0.99989 and 0.9990, respectively. A variational autoencoder revealed four distinct metabolic clusters, and SHAP analysis identified glycolysis, the TCA cycle, and lipid biosynthesis as key biomass determinants. In silico overexpression achieved a biomass flux of 0.979 gDW/hr, while Bayesian optimization of nutrient constraints produced a 12-fold increase (0.0858 to 1.041 gDW/hr). A generative adversarial network proposed stoichiometrically feasible novel flux configurations. This framework demonstrates how genome-scale simulation, interpretable ML, and generative modeling can advance yeast metabolic engineering.
中文标题/摘要
标题：整合基因组尺度代谢建模与机器学习框架用于预测和优化酿酒酵母中生物燃料相关生物质生产
酿酒酵母是工业生物技术中的核心微生物，因其遗传可操作性和强大的发酵能力而备受重视。准确预测不同环境和遗传扰动下的生物质通量仍然是理性菌株设计的重大挑战。我们提出了一个计算框架，将Yeast9基因组尺度代谢模型与机器学习和优化技术相结合，以预测、解释和增强生物质通量。通过改变葡萄糖、氧气和铵盐摄取速率，通量平衡分析生成了2000个通量谱。随机森林和XGBoost回归器分别实现了0.99989和0.9990的R2分数。变分自编码器揭示了四个不同的代谢簇，SHAP分析确定糖酵解、TCA循环和脂质生物合成为关键生物质决定因素。计算机模拟过表达实现了0.979克干重/小时的生物质通量，而通过贝叶斯优化营养约束则使通量提高了12倍（从0.0858增至1.041克干重/小时）。生成对抗网络提出了化学计量学上可行的新型通量配置。该框架展示了基因组尺度模拟、可解释机器学习和生成建模如何推动酵母代谢工程的发展。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of predicting biomass production in Saccharomyces cerevisiae for biofuel applications, this study developed an integrative computational framework combining the Yeast9 genome-scale metabolic model with machine learning and optimization techniques. The method involved generating 2,000 flux profiles via flux balance analysis under varied nutrient conditions, training Random Forest and XGBoost regressors for high-accuracy biomass flux prediction, and employing a variational autoencoder for metabolic clustering alongside SHAP analysis for interpretability. Key experimental results include achieving R2 values up to 0.99989 with machine learning models, identifying glycolysis and the TCA cycle as critical biomass determinants, and optimizing biomass flux through in silico overexpression and Bayesian optimization, which yielded a 12-fold increase from 0.0858 to 1.041 gDW/hr, demonstrating the framework's potential for advancing metabolic engineering.
本研究旨在解决预测酿酒酵母生物质生产以用于生物燃料应用的挑战，开发了一个整合酵母9基因组尺度代谢模型与机器学习和优化技术的计算框架。方法包括通过通量平衡分析在多种营养条件下生成2000个通量分布，训练随机森林和XGBoost回归器进行高精度生物质通量预测，并利用变分自编码器进行代谢聚类及SHAP分析以增强可解释性。主要实验结果包括机器学习模型达到高达0.99989的R2值，识别糖酵解和三羧酸循环为生物质生产的关键决定因素，以及通过计算机模拟过表达和贝叶斯优化将生物质通量从0.0858提高至1.041 gDW/hr，实现了12倍的增长，证明了该框架在推进代谢工程方面的潜力。
Self-Supervised Multisensory Pretraining for Contact-Rich Robot Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Rickmer Krohn, Vignesh Prasad, Gabriele Tiboni, Georgia Chalvatzaki
First: 2025-11-18T12:32:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T14:42:27+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 11 figures, Accepted at RA-L
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Effective contact-rich manipulation requires robots to synergistically leverage vision, force, and proprioception. However, Reinforcement Learning agents struggle to learn in such multisensory settings, especially amidst sensory noise and dynamic changes. We propose MultiSensory Dynamic Pretraining (MSDP), a novel framework for learning expressive multisensory representations tailored for task-oriented policy learning. MSDP is based on masked autoencoding and trains a transformer-based encoder by reconstructing multisensory observations from only a subset of sensor embeddings, leading to cross-modal prediction and sensor fusion. For downstream policy learning, we introduce a novel asymmetric architecture, where a cross-attention mechanism allows the critic to extract dynamic, task-specific features from the frozen embeddings, while the actor receives a stable pooled representation to guide its actions. Our method demonstrates accelerated learning and robust performance under diverse perturbations, including sensor noise, and changes in object dynamics. Evaluations in multiple challenging, contact-rich robot manipulation tasks in simulation and the real world showcase the effectiveness of MSDP. Our approach exhibits strong robustness to perturbations and achieves high success rates on the real robot with as few as 6,000 online interactions, offering a simple yet powerful solution for complex multisensory robotic control. Website: https://msdp-pearl.github.io/
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向接触密集型机器人强化学习的自监督多感官预训练
有效的接触密集型操作要求机器人协同利用视觉、力觉与本体感知。然而，强化学习智能体在此类多感官场景中学习困难，尤其在感官噪声与动态变化环境下。我们提出多感官动态预训练（MSDP），一种为任务导向策略学习定制表达性多感官表征的新框架。MSDP基于掩码自编码技术，通过仅从部分传感器嵌入重建多感官观测来训练基于Transformer的编码器，实现跨模态预测与传感器融合。对于下游策略学习，我们引入一种新颖的非对称架构：其中评论家通过交叉注意力机制从冻结嵌入中提取动态的任务特定特征，而执行器接收稳定的池化表征以指导其动作。我们的方法在多种扰动（包括传感器噪声与物体动力学变化）下展现出加速学习与鲁棒性能。在仿真与真实世界的多个高难度接触密集型机器人操作任务中的评估验证了MSDP的有效性。该方法对扰动具有强鲁棒性，在真实机器人上仅需6000次在线交互即实现高成功率，为复杂多感官机器人控制提供了简洁而强大的解决方案。项目网站：https://msdp-pearl.github.io/
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the challenge of enabling Reinforcement Learning agents to effectively integrate vision, force, and proprioception for contact-rich manipulation, which is difficult due to sensory noise and dynamic changes. The method introduces MultiSensory Dynamic Pretraining (MSDP), a self-supervised framework that uses masked autoencoding with a transformer-based encoder to reconstruct multisensory observations from partial inputs, fostering cross-modal prediction and sensor fusion; for downstream policy learning, it employs an asymmetric architecture where a critic uses cross-attention on frozen embeddings for task-specific features and an actor uses a stable pooled representation. Experimental results in simulation and real-world contact-rich manipulation tasks show that MSDP accelerates learning, provides robust performance under perturbations like sensor noise and object dynamics changes, and achieves high success rates on a real robot with only 6,000 online interactions.
本文的动机是解决强化学习智能体在接触式机器人操作中难以有效整合视觉、力和本体感知的挑战，这主要源于感官噪声和动态变化带来的困难。方法上提出了多感官动态预训练（MSDP），这是一个自监督框架，采用基于掩码自编码的Transformer编码器，通过重建部分传感器嵌入的多感官观测来实现跨模态预测和传感器融合；在下游策略学习中，采用非对称架构，其中评论家通过交叉注意力从冻结嵌入中提取动态任务特征，而执行器使用稳定的池化表示来指导动作。实验结果表明，在仿真和真实世界的多种接触式操作任务中，MSDP能加速学习，在传感器噪声和物体动态变化等扰动下表现出强鲁棒性，并在真实机器人上仅用6000次在线交互就实现了高成功率。
Fitting Reinforcement Learning Model to Behavioral Data under Bandits
Authors: Hao Zhu, Jasper Hoffmann, Baohe Zhang, Joschka Boedecker
Venue: Front. Appl. Math. Stat., 12:1762084, 2026
First: 2025-11-06T15:24:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T14:40:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We consider the problem of fitting a reinforcement learning (RL) model to some given behavioral data under a multi-armed bandit environment. These models have received much attention in recent years for characterizing human and animal decision making behavior. We provide a generic mathematical optimization problem formulation for the fitting problem of a wide range of RL models that appear frequently in scientific research applications. We then provide a detailed theoretical analysis of its convexity properties. Based on the theoretical results, we introduce a novel solution method for the fitting problem of RL models based on convex relaxation and optimization. Our method is then evaluated in several simulated and real-world bandit environments to compare with some benchmark methods that appear in the literature. Numerical results indicate that our method achieves comparable performance to the state-of-the-art, while significantly reducing computation time. We also provide an open-source Python package for our proposed method to empower researchers to apply it in the analysis of their datasets directly, without prior knowledge of convex optimization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：在多臂老虎机环境下将强化学习模型拟合至行为数据
本文研究在多臂老虎机环境中，将强化学习模型拟合至给定行为数据的问题。近年来，这类模型在刻画人类与动物决策行为方面备受关注。我们为科研应用中常见的多种强化学习模型拟合问题，提出了通用的数学优化问题表述，并对其凸性进行了详细理论分析。基于理论结果，我们引入了一种基于凸松弛与优化的新型强化学习模型拟合方法。通过在模拟及真实老虎机环境中的评估，与文献中的基准方法对比表明：该方法在达到先进性能的同时，显著降低了计算时间。我们还提供了开源Python工具包，使研究者无需凸优化先验知识即可直接应用于数据分析。

RetroAgent: From Solving to Evolving via Retrospective Dual Intrinsic Feedback
Authors: Xiaoying Zhang, Zichen Liu, Yipeng Zhang, Xia Hu, Wenqi Shao
First: 2026-03-09T16:23:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T14:07:56+00:00
Comments: 48 pages, with updated results
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Standard reinforcement learning (RL) for large language model (LLM) agents typically optimizes extrinsic rewards, prioritizing isolated task completion over continual adaptation. Consequently, agents often converge to suboptimal policies due to limited exploration. Furthermore, accumulated experience remains implicitly trapped within model parameters, hindering its explicit reuse for guiding future decisions. Inspired by human retrospective self-improvement, we introduce RetroAgent, an online RL framework that trains agents to master complex interactive environments not only by solving tasks, but by evolving under the joint guidance of extrinsic task rewards and retrospective dual intrinsic feedback. Specifically, RetroAgent employs a hindsight self-reflection mechanism that generates two complementary signals: (1) intrinsic numerical feedback, which rewards promising exploration by tracking real-time incremental subtask progress relative to prior attempts; and (2) intrinsic language feedback, which enables explicit experience reuse by distilling reusable lessons into a memory buffer for subsequent decision-making. To effectively leverage these textual experiences, we propose Similarity & Utility-Aware Upper Confidence Bound (SimUtil-UCB), a retrieval strategy that balances relevance, historical utility, and exploration. Extensive experiments across four challenging agentic tasks show that RetroAgent achieves new state-of-the-art (SOTA) performance. Notably, it surpasses Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) baselines by +18.3% on ALFWorld, +15.4% on WebShop, +27.1% on Sokoban, and +8.9% on MineSweeper, while exhibiting strong test-time adaptation and out-of-distribution generalization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：回顾智能体：通过回顾性双重内在反馈实现从求解到演化
针对大语言模型智能体的标准强化学习通常优化外在奖励，优先考虑孤立任务完成而非持续适应，导致智能体常因探索有限而收敛至次优策略。且累积经验隐式留存于模型参数中，阻碍其显式复用以指导未来决策。受人类回顾式自我改进启发，我们提出RetroAgent——一种在线强化学习框架，通过外在任务奖励与回顾性双重内在反馈的联合指导，训练智能体不仅解决任务，更在复杂交互环境中实现演化。具体而言，RetroAgent采用事后自省机制生成两种互补信号：（1）内在数值反馈：通过追踪相较于先前尝试的实时增量子任务进度，奖励有前景的探索；（2）内在语言反馈：将可复用经验提炼至记忆缓冲区以供后续决策，实现显式经验复用。为有效利用文本经验，我们提出相似性与效用感知上置信界检索策略，平衡相关性、历史效用与探索需求。在四项挑战性智能体任务上的实验表明，RetroAgent取得最新最优性能：在ALFWorld超越GRPO基线18.3%、WebShop提升15.4%、Sokoban提高27.1%、MineSweeper改进8.9%，同时展现出强大的测试时适应与分布外泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of standard reinforcement learning for LLM agents, which focuses on extrinsic rewards and lacks mechanisms for explicit experience reuse, this paper introduces RetroAgent, an online RL framework that enhances agent adaptation through retrospective dual intrinsic feedback. The method employs a hindsight self-reflection mechanism generating both intrinsic numerical feedback to reward incremental subtask progress and intrinsic language feedback to distill reusable lessons into a memory buffer, coupled with a SimUtil-UCB retrieval strategy for balanced experience retrieval. Experimental results across four challenging tasks demonstrate state-of-the-art performance, with significant improvements over GRPO baselines, including +18.3% on ALFWorld and +27.1% on Sokoban, alongside strong test-time adaptation and generalization capabilities.
针对标准强化学习在大型语言模型智能体中过度依赖外部奖励、缺乏显式经验复用机制的问题，本文提出了RetroAgent框架，通过回顾式双重内在反馈促进智能体的持续进化。该方法采用事后反思机制，生成内在数值反馈以奖励子任务进展，以及内在语言反馈将可重用经验存入记忆缓冲区，并结合SimUtil-UCB检索策略平衡经验的相关性与效用。在四项挑战性任务上的实验表明，该框架实现了最先进的性能，相比GRPO基线在ALFWorld上提升18.3%，在Sokoban上提升27.1%，同时展现出强大的测试时适应和分布外泛化能力。
Maximum Entropy Behavior Exploration for Sim2Real Zero-Shot Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jiajun Hu, Nuria Armengol Urpi, Jin Cheng, Stelian Coros
First: 2026-03-26T14:07:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T14:07:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Zero-shot reinforcement learning (RL) algorithms aim to learn a family of policies from a reward-free dataset, and recover optimal policies for any reward function directly at test time. Naturally, the quality of the pretraining dataset determines the performance of the recovered policies across tasks. However, pre-collecting a relevant, diverse dataset without prior knowledge of the downstream tasks of interest remains a challenge. In this work, we study $\textit{online}$ zero-shot RL for quadrupedal control on real robotic systems, building upon the Forward-Backward (FB) algorithm. We observe that undirected exploration yields low-diversity data, leading to poor downstream performance and rendering policies impractical for direct hardware deployment. Therefore, we introduce FB-MEBE, an online zero-shot RL algorithm that combines an unsupervised behavior exploration strategy with a regularization critic. FB-MEBE promotes exploration by maximizing the entropy of the achieved behavior distribution. Additionally, a regularization critic shapes the recovered policies toward more natural and physically plausible behaviors. We empirically demonstrate that FB-MEBE achieves and improved performance compared to other exploration strategies in a range of simulated downstream tasks, and that it renders natural policies that can be seamlessly deployed to hardware without further finetuning. Videos and code available on our website.

标题：面向仿真到现实零样本强化学习的最大熵行为探索
零样本强化学习算法旨在从无奖励数据集中学习一组策略，并在测试时直接针对任意奖励函数恢复最优策略。预训练数据集的质量自然决定了恢复策略在不同任务中的性能。然而，在缺乏下游任务先验知识的情况下，预先收集相关且多样化的数据集仍具挑战性。本研究基于前向-后向算法，探索四足机器人控制中的在线零样本强化学习。我们发现无导向探索会产生低多样性数据，导致下游性能不佳，且策略难以直接部署至硬件。为此，我们提出FB-MEBE算法，将无监督行为探索策略与正则化评判器相结合。FB-MEBE通过最大化已实现行为分布的熵来促进探索，同时利用正则化评判器引导恢复策略趋向更自然、物理可行的行为。实验表明，在一系列仿真下游任务中，FB-MEBE相比其他探索策略实现了更优性能，且生成的策略无需微调即可直接部署至硬件。视频与代码已发布于项目网站。

Research on environment perception and behavior prediction of intelligent UAV based on semantic communication
Authors: Kechong Ren, Li Gao, Qi Guan
First: 2025-01-08T13:03:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T13:36:18+00:00

Abstract
The convergence of drone delivery systems, virtual worlds, and blockchain has transformed logistics and supply chain management, providing a fast, and environmentally friendly alternative to traditional ground transportation methods;Provide users with a real-world experience, virtual service providers need to collect up-to-the-minute delivery information from edge devices. To address this challenge, 1) a reinforcement learning approach is introduced to enable drones with fast training capabilities and the ability to autonomously adapt to new virtual scenarios for effective resource allocation.2) A semantic communication framework for meta-universes is proposed, which utilizes the extraction of semantic information to reduce the communication cost and incentivize the transmission of information for meta-universe services.3) In order to ensure that user information security, a lightweight authentication and key agreement scheme is designed between the drone and the user by introducing blockchain technology. In our experiments, the drone adaptation performance is improved by about 35\%, and the local offloading rate can reach 90\% with the increase of the number of base stations. The semantic communication system proposed in this paper is compared with the Cross Entropy baseline model. Introducing blockchain technology the throughput of the transaction is maintained at a stable value with different number of drones.

Modernising Reinforcement Learning-Based Navigation for Embodied Semantic Scene Graph Generation
Authors: Roman Kueble, Marco Hueller, Mrunmai Phatak, Rainer Lienhart, Joerg Haehner
First: 2026-03-26T13:10:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T13:10:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Semantic world models enable embodied agents to reason about objects, relations, and spatial context beyond purely geometric representations. In Organic Computing, such models are a key enabler for objective-driven self-adaptation under uncertainty and resource constraints. The core challenge is to acquire observations maximising model quality and downstream usefulness within a limited action budget. Semantic scene graphs (SSGs) provide a structured and compact representation for this purpose. However, constructing them within a finite action horizon requires exploration strategies that trade off information gain against navigation cost and decide when additional actions yield diminishing returns. This work presents a modular navigation component for Embodied Semantic Scene Graph Generation and modernises its decision-making by replacing the policy-optimisation method and revisiting the discrete action formulation. We study compact and finer-grained, larger discrete motion sets and compare a single-head policy over atomic actions with a factorised multi-head policy over action components. We evaluate curriculum learning and optional depth-based collision supervision, and assess SSG completeness, execution safety, and navigation behaviour. Results show that replacing the optimisation algorithm alone improves SSG completeness by 21\% relative to the baseline under identical reward shaping. Depth mainly affects execution safety (collision-free motion), while completeness remains largely unchanged. Combining modern optimisation with a finer-grained, factorised action representation yields the strongest overall completeness--efficiency trade-off.

标题：面向具身语义场景图生成的强化学习导航方法现代化
语义世界模型使具身智能体能够基于超越纯几何表征的对象、关系和空间上下文进行推理。在有机计算中，此类模型是在不确定性和资源约束下实现目标驱动自适应能力的关键支撑。核心挑战在于如何在有限行动预算内获取能最大化模型质量与下游应用价值的观测数据。语义场景图为这一目标提供了结构化紧凑表征，但在有限行动范围内构建此类图谱需要探索策略，以权衡信息增益与导航成本，并判断何时额外行动将产生收益递减效应。本研究提出了面向具身语义场景图生成的模块化导航组件，通过替换策略优化方法并重构离散行动表述来实现决策机制现代化。我们研究了紧凑型与细粒度大规模离散运动集合，比较了原子动作的单头策略与动作组件的分解式多头策略。评估了课程学习与可选的基于深度的碰撞监督机制，并对语义场景图完整性、执行安全性和导航行为进行了量化分析。结果表明：在相同奖励塑造条件下，仅替换优化算法即可使场景图完整性相对基线提升21%；深度信息主要影响执行安全性（无碰撞运动），而完整性基本保持不变；现代优化算法与细粒度分解式动作表征的结合，实现了最优的整体完整性-效率权衡。

The method modernizes the navigation component for embodied SSG generation by replacing the policy-optimization algorithm and exploring discrete action formulations, including comparing atomic versus factorized multi-head policies over action components, while also evaluating curriculum learning and depth-based collision supervision. Experimental results demonstrate that updating the optimization algorithm alone improves SSG completeness by 21% relative to the baseline, depth supervision primarily enhances execution safety by reducing collisions without affecting completeness, and the combination of modern optimization with a finer-grained, factorized action representation achieves the best overall trade-off between completeness and efficiency.

P^2O: Joint Policy and Prompt Optimization
Authors: Xinyu Lu, Kaiqi Zhang, Jinglin Yang, Boxi Cao, Yaojie Lu, Hongyu Lin, Min He, Xianpei Han, Le Sun
First: 2026-03-23T12:08:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T12:57:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has emerged as a powerful paradigm for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, vanilla RLVR suffers from inefficient exploration, particularly when confronting "hard samples" that yield nearzero success rates. In such scenarios, the reliance on sparse outcome rewards typically results in zero-advantage estimates, effectively starving the model of supervision signals despite the high informational value of these instances. To address this, we propose P^2O, a novel framework that synergizes Prompt Optimization with Policy Optimization. P^2O identifies hard samples during training iterations and leverages the GeneticPareto (GEPA) prompt optimization algorithm to evolve prompt templates that guide the model toward discovering successful trajectories. Crucially, unlike traditional prompt engineering methods that rely on input augmentation, P^2O distills the reasoning gains induced by these optimized prompts directly into the model parameters. This mechanism provides denser positive supervision signals for hard samples and accelerates convergence. Extensive experiments demonstrate that P^2O not only achieves superior performance on in-distribution datasets but also exhibits strong generalization, yielding substantial improvements on out-of-distribution benchmarks (+4.7% avg.).
中文标题/摘要
标题：P^2O：联合策略与提示优化
基于可验证奖励的强化学习已成为增强大语言模型推理能力的重要范式。然而，传统RLVR存在探索效率低下的问题，尤其在面对成功率趋近于零的“困难样本”时。此类场景下，稀疏结果奖励通常导致优势估计为零，使模型难以从这些高信息价值样本中获得有效监督信号。为此，我们提出P^2O框架，将提示优化与策略优化协同整合。该框架在训练迭代中识别困难样本，并利用遗传帕累托提示优化算法进化提示模板，引导模型发现成功轨迹。与传统依赖输入增强的提示工程方法不同，P^2O将优化提示产生的推理增益直接蒸馏至模型参数中。该机制为困难样本提供更密集的正向监督信号，加速收敛过程。大量实验表明，P^2O不仅在分布内数据集上取得更优性能，还展现出强大的泛化能力，在分布外基准测试中实现显著提升（平均+4.7%）。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the inefficient exploration problem in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) for Large Language Models, particularly when dealing with hard samples that yield near-zero success rates and sparse rewards. To solve this, the authors propose P^2O, a framework that jointly optimizes policy and prompts by identifying hard samples during training and using a GeneticPareto algorithm to evolve prompt templates that guide the model toward successful trajectories, then distilling these reasoning gains into model parameters for denser supervision. Experimental results show that P^2O achieves superior in-distribution performance and strong generalization, with an average improvement of +4.7% on out-of-distribution benchmarks.
该论文针对大型语言模型的可验证奖励强化学习中探索效率低下的问题，特别是在处理成功率极低、奖励稀疏的困难样本时。为解决此问题，作者提出了P^2O框架，通过联合优化策略和提示，在训练中识别困难样本，并利用遗传帕累托算法进化提示模板以引导模型发现成功轨迹，然后将这些推理收益蒸馏到模型参数中以提供更密集的监督信号。实验结果表明，P^2O在分布内数据集上取得了更优性能，并展现出强大的泛化能力，在分布外基准测试中平均提升了4.7%。
Integrating Deep RL and Bayesian Inference for ObjectNav in Mobile Robotics
Authors: João Castelo-Branco, José Santos-Victor, Alexandre Bernardino
First: 2026-03-26T12:15:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T12:15:12+00:00
Comments: Accepted and to be published in the ICARSC 2026 26th IEEE International Conference on Autonomous Robot Systems and Competitions
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autonomous object search is challenging for mobile robots operating in indoor environments due to partial observability, perceptual uncertainty, and the need to trade off exploration and navigation efficiency. Classical probabilistic approaches explicitly represent uncertainty but typically rely on handcrafted action-selection heuristics, while deep reinforcement learning enables adaptive policies but often suffers from slow convergence and limited interpretability. This paper proposes a hybrid object-search framework that integrates Bayesian inference with deep reinforcement learning. The method maintains a spatial belief map over target locations, updated online through Bayesian inference from calibrated object detections, and trains a reinforcement learning policy to select navigation actions directly from this probabilistic representation. The approach is evaluated in realistic indoor simulation using Habitat 3.0 and compared against developed baseline strategies. Across two indoor environments, the proposed method improves success rate while reducing search effort. Overall, the results support the value of combining Bayesian belief estimation with learned action selection to achieve more efficient and reliable objectsearch behavior under partial observability.

标题：移动机器人目标导航中深度强化学习与贝叶斯推理的融合研究
室内环境中移动机器人的自主目标搜索面临局部可观测性、感知不确定性及探索与导航效率权衡等挑战。经典概率方法虽能显式表征不确定性，但通常依赖人工设计的动作选择启发式规则；深度强化学习可实现自适应策略，但常存在收敛缓慢和可解释性有限的问题。本文提出一种融合贝叶斯推理与深度强化学习的混合目标搜索框架：通过校准目标检测的贝叶斯推理在线更新目标位置的空间置信度地图，并训练强化学习策略直接基于该概率表征选择导航动作。在Habitat 3.0仿真环境中与基线策略的对比实验表明，该方法在两种室内场景中均能提升成功率并降低搜索成本。研究结果验证了贝叶斯置信估计与学习型动作选择相结合，能在局部可观测条件下实现更高效可靠的目标搜索行为。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of autonomous object search for mobile robots in indoor environments, where partial observability and perceptual uncertainty complicate efficient exploration. The authors propose a hybrid framework that integrates Bayesian inference with deep reinforcement learning, maintaining a spatial belief map over target locations updated via Bayesian inference from object detections and training an RL policy to select navigation actions from this probabilistic representation. Experimental evaluation in realistic indoor simulations using Habitat 3.0 shows that the method improves success rates and reduces search effort compared to baseline strategies, demonstrating the value of combining Bayesian belief estimation with learned action selection for more efficient and reliable object search under partial observability.

TimeLens: Rethinking Video Temporal Grounding with Multimodal LLMs
Authors: Jun Zhang, Teng Wang, Yuying Ge, Yixiao Ge, Xinhao Li, Ying Shan, Limin Wang
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2025-12-16T18:59:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T11:38:43+00:00
Comments: CVPR 2026. Website: https://timelens-arc-lab.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
This paper does not introduce a novel method but instead establishes a straightforward, incremental, yet essential baseline for video temporal grounding (VTG), a core capability in video understanding. While multimodal large language models (MLLMs) excel at various video understanding tasks, the recipes for optimizing them for VTG remain under-explored. In this paper, we present TimeLens, a systematic investigation into building MLLMs with strong VTG ability, along two primary dimensions: data quality and algorithmic design. We first expose critical quality issues in existing VTG benchmarks and introduce TimeLens-Bench, comprising meticulously re-annotated versions of three popular benchmarks with strict quality criteria. Our analysis reveals dramatic model re-rankings compared to legacy benchmarks, confirming the unreliability of prior evaluation standards. We also address noisy training data through an automated re-annotation pipeline, yielding TimeLens-100K, a large-scale, high-quality training dataset. Building on our data foundation, we conduct in-depth explorations of algorithmic design principles, yielding a series of meaningful insights and effective yet efficient practices. These include interleaved textual encoding for time representation, a thinking-free reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) approach as the training paradigm, and carefully designed recipes for RLVR training. These efforts culminate in TimeLens models, a family of MLLMs with state-of-the-art VTG performance among open-source models and even surpass proprietary models such as GPT-5 and Gemini-2.5-Flash. All codes, data, and models will be released to facilitate future research.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TimeLens：基于多模态大语言模型的视频时序定位方法再思考
本文未提出全新方法，而是为视频理解的核心能力——视频时序定位（VTG）建立了一个简明、渐进但至关重要的基线。尽管多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在多种视频理解任务中表现卓越，但针对VTG的优化方案仍待深入探索。本研究提出TimeLens，从数据质量与算法设计两个维度系统探究构建具备强VTG能力的MLLMs。我们首先揭示现有VTG基准数据集的关键质量问题，并推出TimeLens-Bench——包含三个经严格质量标准重新标注的流行基准版本。分析表明，相较于传统基准，模型排名发生显著变化，证实了既往评估标准的不可靠性。同时，我们通过自动重标注流程处理噪声训练数据，构建了大规模高质量训练数据集TimeLens-100K。基于此数据基础，我们深入探索算法设计原则，获得一系列重要洞见与高效实践方案，包括：用于时间表征的交错文本编码、采用可验证奖励的无思维强化学习（RLVR）训练范式，以及精心设计的RLVR训练方案。这些工作最终催生出TimeLens模型系列——该系列开源MLLMs在VTG性能上达到业界领先水平，甚至超越GPT-5与Gemini-2.5-Flash等专有模型。所有代码、数据与模型均将开源以促进后续研究。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the under-explored optimization of multimodal large language models (MLLMs) for video temporal grounding (VTG), this paper introduces TimeLens as a systematic baseline study focusing on data quality and algorithmic design. The method involves creating high-quality benchmarks (TimeLens-Bench) and a large-scale training dataset (TimeLens-100K) through re-annotation, alongside exploring algorithmic principles such as interleaved textual time encoding and a reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) training paradigm. Experimental results show that the resulting TimeLens models achieve state-of-the-art VTG performance among open-source models and even surpass proprietary models like GPT-5 and Gemini-2.5-Flash, with all resources released to support future research.

SpecXMaster Technical Report
Authors: Yutang Ge, Yaning Cui, Hanzheng Li, Jun-Jie Wang, Fanjie Xu, Jinhan Dong, Yongqi Jin, Dongxu Cui, Peng Jin, Guojiang Zhao, Hengxing Cai, Rong Zhu, Linfeng Zhang, Xiaohong Ji, Zhifeng Gao
First: 2026-03-24T11:49:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T11:20:14+00:00
Comments: Technical report from DP Technology.22 pages, 7 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Intelligent spectroscopy serves as a pivotal element in AI-driven closed-loop scientific discovery, functioning as the critical bridge between matter structure and artificial intelligence. However, conventional expert-dependent spectral interpretation encounters substantial hurdles, including susceptibility to human bias and error, dependence on limited specialized expertise, and variability across interpreters. To address these challenges, we propose SpecXMaster, an intelligent framework leveraging Agentic Reinforcement Learning (RL) for NMR molecular spectral interpretation. SpecXMaster enables automated extraction of multiplicity information from both 1H and 13C spectra directly from raw FID (free induction decay) data. This end-to-end pipeline enables fully automated interpretation of NMR spectra into chemical structures. It demonstrates superior performance across multiple public NMR interpretation benchmarks and has been refined through iterative evaluations by professional chemical spectroscopists. We believe that SpecXMaster, as a novel methodological paradigm for spectral interpretation, will have a profound impact on the organic chemistry community.

Macroscopic Characteristics of Mixed Traffic Flow with Deep Reinforcement Learning Based Automated and Human-Driven Vehicles
Authors: Pankaj Kumar, Pranamesh Chakraborty, Subrahmanya Swamy Peruru
First: 2026-03-26T11:14:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T11:14:20+00:00
Comments: Total 5 figures and 2 table
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Automated Vehicle (AV) control in mixed traffic, where AVs coexist with human-driven vehicles, poses significant challenges in balancing safety, efficiency, comfort, fuel efficiency, and compliance with traffic rules while capturing heterogeneous driver behavior. Traditional car-following models, such as the Intelligent Driver Model (IDM), often struggle to generalize across diverse traffic scenarios and typically do not account for fuel efficiency, motivating the use of learning-based approaches. Although Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) has shown strong microscopic performance in car-following conditions, its macroscopic traffic flow characteristics remain underexplored. This study focuses on analyzing the macroscopic traffic flow characteristics and fuel efficiency of DRL-based models in mixed traffic. A Twin Delayed Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient (TD3) algorithm is implemented for AVs' control and trained using the NGSIM highway dataset, enabling realistic interaction with human-driven vehicles. Traffic performance is evaluated using the Fundamental Diagram (FD) under varying driver heterogeneity, heterogeneous time-gap penetration levels, and different shares of RL-controlled vehicles. A macroscopic level comparison of fuel efficiency between the RL-based AV model and the IDM is also conducted. Results show that traffic performance is sensitive to the distribution of safe time gaps and the proportion of RL vehicles. Transitioning from fully human-driven to fully RL-controlled traffic can increase road capacity by approximately 7.52%. Further, RL-based AVs also improve average fuel efficiency by about 28.98% at higher speeds (above 50 km/h), and by 1.86% at lower speeds (below 50 km/h) compared to the IDM. Overall, the DRL framework enhances traffic capacity and fuel efficiency without compromising safety.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于深度强化学习的自动驾驶与人工驾驶混合交通流宏观特性研究
在自动驾驶车辆（AV）与人工驾驶车辆共存的混合交通中，AV控制面临平衡安全性、效率、舒适性、燃油经济性及交通规则遵守等多重挑战，同时需应对异质驾驶行为。传统跟驰模型（如智能驾驶员模型IDM）常难以泛化至多样交通场景，且通常未考虑燃油经济性，这推动了基于学习方法的应用。尽管深度强化学习（DRL）在微观跟驰场景中表现优异，其宏观交通流特性尚未充分探索。本研究聚焦于分析基于DRL的模型在混合交通中的宏观交通流特性与燃油经济性。采用双延迟深度确定性策略梯度（TD3）算法控制AV，并利用NGSIM高速公路数据集进行训练，以实现与人工驾驶车辆的真实交互。通过基本图（FD）评估不同驾驶异质性、异质时距渗透水平及RL控制车辆占比下的交通性能，并对基于RL的AV模型与IDM进行宏观燃油经济性比较。结果表明：交通性能对安全时距分布和RL车辆比例敏感；从全人工驾驶过渡至全RL控制交通可使道路通行能力提升约7.52%；与IDM相比，基于RL的AV在较高速度（>50 km/h）下平均燃油经济性提升约28.98%，在较低速度（<50 km/h）下提升1.86%。总体而言，DRL框架在保障安全的同时提升了通行能力与燃油经济性。
Summary / 总结
This study is motivated by the challenges of controlling Automated Vehicles (AVs) in mixed traffic with human-driven vehicles, where traditional models like the Intelligent Driver Model (IDM) often fail to generalize across scenarios or optimize fuel efficiency, prompting the adoption of learning-based approaches. The method employs a Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) framework, specifically the Twin Delayed Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient (TD3) algorithm, trained on the NGSIM highway dataset to control AVs and simulate interactions with human drivers, with macroscopic traffic flow and fuel efficiency analyzed under varying conditions of driver heterogeneity, time-gap penetration, and AV proportions. Experimental results reveal that traffic performance depends on safe time-gap distributions and RL vehicle shares, with a transition to fully RL-controlled traffic increasing road capacity by about 7.52% and improving average fuel efficiency by approximately 28.98% at higher speeds and 1.86% at lower speeds compared to IDM, demonstrating enhanced capacity and fuel efficiency without safety compromises.

Practical Efficient Global Optimization is No-regret
Authors: Jingyi Wang, Haowei Wang, Nai-Yuan Chiang, Juliane Mueller, Tucker Hartland, Cosmin G. Petra
First: 2026-03-26T10:58:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T10:58:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Efficient global optimization (EGO) is one of the most widely used noise-free Bayesian optimization algorithms.It comprises the Gaussian process (GP) surrogate model and expected improvement (EI) acquisition function. In practice, when EGO is applied, a scalar matrix of a small positive value (also called a nugget or jitter) is usually added to the covariance matrix of the deterministic GP to improve numerical stability. We refer to this EGO with a positive nugget as the practical EGO. Despite its wide adoption and empirical success, to date, cumulative regret bounds for practical EGO have yet to be established. In this paper, we present for the first time the cumulative regret upper bound of practical EGO. In particular, we show that practical EGO has sublinear cumulative regret bounds and thus is a no-regret algorithm for commonly used kernels including the squared exponential (SE) and Matérn kernels ($ν>\frac{1}{2}$). Moreover, we analyze the effect of the nugget on the regret bound and discuss the theoretical implication on its choice. Numerical experiments are conducted to support and validate our findings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：实用高效全局优化算法具有无遗憾特性
高效全局优化（EGO）是最广泛使用的无噪声贝叶斯优化算法之一，由高斯过程（GP）代理模型和期望提升（EI）采集函数构成。实际应用中，为提升数值稳定性，通常在确定性GP协方差矩阵中添加小正值的标量矩阵（亦称块金或抖动项）。我们将这种含正块金项的EGO称为实用EGO。尽管该算法已被广泛采用且经验验证有效，但迄今为止其实用版本的累积遗憾界尚未建立。本文首次提出了实用EGO的累积遗憾上界，证明其对常用核函数（包括平方指数核与Matérn核，其中ν>1/2）具有次线性累积遗憾界，因而属于无遗憾算法。此外，我们分析了块金项对遗憾界的影响，并讨论了其选择的理论意义。数值实验验证了研究结论。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the lack of theoretical regret guarantees for the widely used Efficient Global Optimization (EGO) algorithm when implemented with a numerical nugget for stability, a common practical necessity. By analyzing this 'practical EGO' variant with Gaussian process surrogates and the expected improvement acquisition function, the authors establish, for the first time, sublinear cumulative regret bounds, proving it is a no-regret algorithm for standard kernels like squared exponential and Matérn. Their theoretical analysis, supported by numerical experiments, also examines how the nugget's value influences the regret bound, providing guidance for its practical selection.
本文针对实践中为提升数值稳定性而广泛采用的、添加了数值扰动项的实用高效全局优化算法，解决了其缺乏理论遗憾界保证的问题。通过分析这种采用高斯过程代理模型和期望提升采集函数的'实用EGO'变体，作者首次建立了次线性累积遗憾上界，证明其对常用核函数如平方指数核和Matérn核是一个无遗憾算法。理论分析还探讨了扰动值对遗憾界的影响，为实际选择提供了依据，并通过数值实验验证了研究结果。
Physics-Informed Evolution: An Evolutionary Framework for Solving Quantum Control Problems Involving the Schrödinger Equation
Authors: Kaichen Ouyang, Mingyang Yu, Zong Ke, Jun Zhang, Yi Chen, Huiling Chen
First: 2025-02-06T08:43:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T10:35:58+00:00
Comments: 17 pages, 4 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Physics-informed Neural Networks (PINNs) show that embedding physical laws directly into the learning objective can significantly enhance the efficiency and physical consistency of neural network solutions. Similar to optimizing loss functions in machine learning, evolutionary algorithms iteratively optimize objective functions by simulating natural selection processes. Inspired by this principle, we ask a natural question: can physical information be similarly embedded into the fitness function of evolutionary algorithms? In this work, we propose Physics-informed Evolution (PIE), a novel framework that incorporates physical information derived from governing physical laws into the evolutionary fitness landscape, thereby extending Physics-informed artificial intelligence methods from machine learning to the broader domain of evolutionary computation. As a concrete instantiation, we apply PIE to quantum control problems governed by the Schrödinger equation, where the goal is to find optimal control fields that drive quantum systems from initial states to desired target states. We validate PIE on three representative quantum control benchmarks: state preparation in V-type three-level systems, entangled state generation in superconducting quantum circuits, and two-atom cavity QED systems. Within the PIE framework, we systematically compare the performance of ten single-objective and five multi-objective evolutionary algorithms. Experimental results demonstrate that by embedding physical information into the fitness function, PIE effectively guides evolutionary search, yielding control fields with high fidelity, low state deviation, and robust performance across different scenarios. Our findings further suggest that the Physics-informed principle extends naturally beyond neural network training to the broader domain of evolutionary computation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：物理信息进化：一种求解含薛定谔方程量子控制问题的进化框架
物理信息神经网络（PINNs）表明，将物理定律直接嵌入学习目标可显著提升神经网络解的效率和物理一致性。类似于机器学习中优化损失函数，进化算法通过模拟自然选择过程迭代优化目标函数。受此启发，我们提出一个自然问题：物理信息能否类似地嵌入进化算法的适应度函数？本文提出物理信息进化（PIE）这一新颖框架，将基于主导物理定律的物理信息融入进化适应度景观，从而将物理信息人工智能方法从机器学习拓展至更广泛的进化计算领域。作为具体实例，我们将PIE应用于薛定谔方程描述的量子控制问题，其目标是寻找驱动量子系统从初始态演化至目标态的最优控制场。我们在三个代表性量子控制基准上验证PIE：V型三能级系统的态制备、超导量子电路中的纠缠态生成，以及双原子腔QED系统。在PIE框架内，我们系统比较了十种单目标与五种多目标进化算法的性能。实验结果表明，通过将物理信息嵌入适应度函数，PIE能有效引导进化搜索，产生具有高保真度、低态偏差且跨场景性能稳健的控制场。我们的发现进一步表明，物理信息原则可自然延伸至神经网络训练之外，适用于更广泛的进化计算领域。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the success of Physics-informed Neural Networks (PINNs) in embedding physical laws into machine learning, this work explores whether similar principles can enhance evolutionary algorithms by incorporating physical information into their fitness functions. The proposed Physics-informed Evolution (PIE) framework integrates governing physical laws, specifically the Schrödinger equation, into the evolutionary fitness landscape to solve quantum control problems, aiming to find optimal control fields that transition quantum systems from initial to target states. Experimental validation on three quantum control benchmarks—state preparation in V-type three-level systems, entangled state generation in superconducting circuits, and two-atom cavity QED systems—demonstrates that PIE effectively guides evolutionary search, yielding high-fidelity, low-deviation control fields with robust performance across scenarios, as shown through comparisons of ten single-objective and five multi-objective evolutionary algorithms.
受物理信息神经网络（PINNs）将物理定律嵌入机器学习目标的启发，本研究探讨了是否可将类似原理应用于进化算法，通过将物理信息融入适应度函数来提升性能。提出的物理信息进化（PIE）框架将薛定谔方程等物理定律整合到进化适应度景观中，以解决量子控制问题，目标是寻找使量子系统从初始态演化到目标态的最优控制场。在三个代表性量子控制基准（V型三能级系统的态制备、超导量子电路中的纠缠态生成以及双原子腔QED系统）上的实验验证表明，PIE能有效引导进化搜索，通过比较十种单目标和五种多目标进化算法，产生了高保真度、低偏差且具有鲁棒性的控制场。
Offline Decision Transformers for Neural Combinatorial Optimization: Surpassing Heuristics on the Traveling Salesman Problem
Authors: Hironori Ohigashi, Shinichiro Hamada
Venue: NeurIPS 2025
First: 2026-03-26T09:47:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T09:47:22+00:00
Comments: 11 pages, 1 figures. Accepted at NeurIPS 2025 Workshop on DiffCoALG
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Combinatorial optimization problems like the Traveling Salesman Problem are critical in industry yet NP-hard. Neural Combinatorial Optimization has shown promise, but its reliance on online reinforcement learning (RL) hampers deployment and underutilizes decades of algorithmic knowledge. We address these limitations by applying the offline RL framework, Decision Transformer, to learn superior strategies directly from datasets of heuristic solutions; it aims to not only to imitate but to synthesize and outperform them. Concretely, we (i) integrate a Pointer Network to handle the instance-dependent, variable action space of node selection, and (ii) employ expectile regression for optimistic conditioning of Return-to-Go, which is crucial for instances with widely varying optimal values. Experiments show that our method consistently produces higher-quality tours than the four classical heuristics it is trained on, demonstrating the potential of offline RL to unlock and exceed the performance embedded in existing domain knowledge.
中文标题/摘要
标题：用于神经组合优化的离线决策变换器：在旅行商问题上超越启发式算法
旅行商问题等组合优化问题在工业中至关重要但属于NP难问题。神经组合优化已展现出潜力，但其对在线强化学习的依赖限制了部署能力，且未能充分利用数十年的算法知识积累。我们通过应用离线强化学习框架——决策变换器，直接从启发式解的数据集中学习更优策略，旨在不仅模仿更能综合并超越这些启发式方法。具体而言，我们（i）集成指针网络以处理节点选择中依赖实例的可变动作空间；（ii）采用期望分位数回归对“收益目标”进行乐观条件化处理，这对最优值差异巨大的问题实例至关重要。实验表明，我们的方法在训练所基于的四种经典启发式算法上均能持续生成更高质量的路径，证明了离线强化学习在挖掘并超越现有领域知识中蕴含性能的潜力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of online reinforcement learning in neural combinatorial optimization, which hinders deployment and underutilizes existing heuristic knowledge, this paper applies the offline Decision Transformer framework to learn from datasets of heuristic solutions for the Traveling Salesman Problem. The method integrates a Pointer Network to manage the variable action space of node selection and uses expectile regression for optimistic conditioning of Return-to-Go, enabling it to synthesize strategies beyond mere imitation. Experimental results demonstrate that the approach consistently generates higher-quality tours than the four classical heuristics it was trained on, showcasing the potential of offline reinforcement learning to surpass embedded domain knowledge.
针对神经组合优化中在线强化学习部署困难且未能充分利用现有启发式知识的问题，本文采用离线决策变换器框架，直接从旅行商问题的启发式解数据集中学习策略。该方法整合了指针网络以处理节点选择中依赖实例的可变动作空间，并采用期望分位数回归对返回目标进行乐观条件化，从而能够合成超越单纯模仿的策略。实验结果表明，该方法生成的路径质量始终优于其训练所用的四种经典启发式算法，证明了离线强化学习在超越现有领域知识性能方面的潜力。
Scalable Multi-Objective Reinforcement Learning with Fairness Guarantees using Lorenz Dominance
Authors: Dimitris Michailidis, Willem Röpke, Diederik M. Roijers, Sennay Ghebreab, Fernando P. Santos
Venue: Journal of Artificial Intelligence Research, Vol. 85, Article 31. Publication date: March 2026
First: 2024-11-27T10:16:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T09:37:38+00:00
Comments: 32 pages. Published in Journal of Artificial Intelligence Research, Vol. 85, Article 31
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-Objective Reinforcement Learning (MORL) aims to learn a set of policies that optimize trade-offs between multiple, often conflicting objectives. MORL is computationally more complex than single-objective RL, particularly as the number of objectives increases. Additionally, when objectives involve the preferences of agents or groups, incorporating fairness becomes both important and socially desirable. This paper introduces a principled algorithm that incorporates fairness into MORL while improving scalability to many-objective problems. We propose using Lorenz dominance to identify policies with equitable reward distributions and introduce lambda-Lorenz dominance to enable flexible fairness preferences. We release a new, large-scale real-world transport planning environment and demonstrate that our method encourages the discovery of fair policies, showing improved scalability in two large cities (Xi'an and Amsterdam). Our methods outperform common multi-objective approaches, particularly in high-dimensional objective spaces.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于洛伦兹占优的可扩展多目标强化学习及其公平性保证
多目标强化学习旨在学习一组策略，以优化多个常相互冲突目标间的权衡。相比单目标强化学习，其计算复杂度更高，尤其在目标数量增加时。当目标涉及智能体或群体的偏好时，纳入公平性既重要又符合社会期望。本文提出一种将公平性融入多目标强化学习的原理性算法，同时提升对多目标问题的可扩展性。我们采用洛伦兹占优识别具有公平奖励分布的策略，并引入λ-洛伦兹占优以实现灵活公平偏好。我们发布了一个新的大规模真实世界交通规划环境，并在西安和阿姆斯特丹两个大城市中验证了本方法能促进公平策略的发现，展现出更优的可扩展性。本方法在多个基准测试中优于常见多目标方法，尤其在高维目标空间中表现突出。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the computational complexity and fairness challenges in Multi-Objective Reinforcement Learning (MORL) by introducing a scalable algorithm that integrates fairness guarantees. The method employs Lorenz dominance to identify policies with equitable reward distributions and proposes lambda-Lorenz dominance to allow flexible fairness preferences. Experimental results on a new large-scale transport planning environment demonstrate that the approach effectively discovers fair policies and improves scalability in many-objective settings, outperforming common MORL methods in cities like Xi'an and Amsterdam.
本文针对多目标强化学习中的计算复杂性和公平性问题，提出了一种可扩展且保证公平性的算法。该方法采用洛伦兹优势来识别具有公平奖励分配的策略，并引入λ-洛伦兹优势以实现灵活的公平衡量偏好。在一个新的大规模交通规划环境中的实验结果表明，该方法能有效发现公平策略，并在西安和阿姆斯特丹等城市的许多目标场景中提高了可扩展性，性能优于常见的多目标方法。
Train at Moving Edge: Online-Verified Prompt Selection for Efficient RL Training of Large Reasoning Model
Authors: Jiahao Wu, Ning Lu, Shengcai Liu, Kun Wang, Yanting Yang, Li Qing, Ke Tang
First: 2026-03-26T08:52:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T08:52:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has become essential for post-training large language models (LLMs) in reasoning tasks. While scaling rollouts can stabilize training and enhance performance, the computational overhead is a critical issue. In algorithms like GRPO, multiple rollouts per prompt incur prohibitive costs, as a large portion of prompts provide negligible gradients and are thus of low utility. To address this problem, we investigate how to select high-utility prompts before the rollout phase. Our experimental analysis reveals that sample utility is non-uniform and evolving: the strongest learning signals concentrate at the ``learning edge", the intersection of intermediate difficulty and high uncertainty, which shifts as training proceeds. Motivated by this, we propose HIVE (History-Informed and online-VErified prompt selection), a dual-stage framework for data-efficient RL. HIVE utilizes historical reward trajectories for coarse selection and employs prompt entropy as a real-time proxy to prune instances with stale utility. By evaluating HIVE across multiple math reasoning benchmarks and models, we show that HIVE yields significant rollout efficiency without compromising performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：移动边缘训练：面向大型推理模型高效强化学习的在线验证提示选择方法
强化学习已成为大型语言模型在推理任务中进行后训练的关键技术。虽然扩展推演规模能稳定训练并提升性能，但其计算开销是核心瓶颈。在GRPO等算法中，每个提示的多轮推演会产生极高成本，因为大量提示提供的梯度可忽略不计，效用低下。为解决该问题，我们研究如何在推演阶段前筛选高效用提示。实验分析表明样本效用具有非均匀且动态演化的特性：最强的学习信号集中在'学习边缘'——即中等难度与高不确定性的交汇区域，该区域会随训练进程移动。基于此发现，我们提出HIVE（历史信息与在线验证的提示选择框架），一种面向数据高效强化学习的双阶段框架。HIVE利用历史奖励轨迹进行粗筛选，并采用提示熵作为实时代理指标来剔除效用衰减的实例。通过在多个数学推理基准和模型上的评估，证明HIVE能在保持性能的同时显著提升推演效率。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the prohibitive computational cost of generating multiple rollouts per prompt in reinforcement learning (RL) for training large reasoning models, as many prompts yield negligible learning gradients. The proposed method, HIVE, is a dual-stage framework that selects high-utility prompts by first using historical reward trajectories for coarse selection and then employing prompt entropy as a real-time proxy to prune instances with stale utility, targeting the shifting "learning edge" of intermediate difficulty and high uncertainty. Main experimental results across multiple math reasoning benchmarks and models demonstrate that HIVE achieves significant improvements in rollout efficiency without compromising model performance.
本研究的动机是解决在大型推理模型的强化学习训练中，每个提示生成多次模拟所导致的过高计算成本问题，因为许多提示产生的学习梯度微乎其微。所提出的方法HIVE是一个双阶段框架，通过首先利用历史奖励轨迹进行粗选，然后采用提示熵作为实时代理来剔除效用过时的实例，从而选择高效用提示，其目标是针对训练过程中不断变化的、具有中等难度和高不确定性的“学习边缘”。在多个数学推理基准和模型上的主要实验结果表明，HIVE在不影响模型性能的前提下，显著提高了模拟效率。
Reinforcement learning for quantum processes with memory
Authors: Josep Lumbreras, Ruo Cheng Huang, Yanglin Hu, Marco Fanizza, Mile Gu
First: 2026-03-26T07:58:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T07:58:13+00:00
Comments: 85 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In reinforcement learning, an agent interacts sequentially with an environment to maximize a reward, receiving only partial, probabilistic feedback. This creates a fundamental exploration-exploitation trade-off: the agent must explore to learn the hidden dynamics while exploiting this knowledge to maximize its target objective. While extensively studied classically, applying this framework to quantum systems requires dealing with hidden quantum states that evolve via unknown dynamics. We formalize this problem via a framework where the environment maintains a hidden quantum memory evolving via unknown quantum channels, and the agent intervenes sequentially using quantum instruments. For this setting, we adapt an optimistic maximum-likelihood estimation algorithm. We extend the analysis to continuous action spaces, allowing us to model general positive operator-valued measures (POVMs). By controlling the propagation of estimation errors through quantum channels and instruments, we prove that the cumulative regret of our strategy scales as $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(\sqrt{K})$ over $K$ episodes. Furthermore, via a reduction to the multi-armed quantum bandit problem, we establish information-theoretic lower bounds demonstrating that this sublinear scaling is strictly optimal up to polylogarithmic factors. As a physical application, we consider state-agnostic work extraction. When extracting free energy from a sequence of non-i.i.d. quantum states correlated by a hidden memory, any lack of knowledge about the source leads to thermodynamic dissipation. In our setting, the mathematical regret exactly quantifies this cumulative dissipation. Using our adaptive algorithm, the agent uses past energy outcomes to improve its extraction protocol on the fly, achieving sublinear cumulative dissipation, and, consequently, an asymptotically zero dissipation rate.
中文标题/摘要
标题：具有记忆的量子过程强化学习
在强化学习中，智能体通过与环境顺序交互以最大化奖励，仅接收部分概率性反馈。这产生了根本性的探索-利用权衡：智能体必须探索以学习隐藏的动态，同时利用这些知识最大化其目标。虽然经典框架已被广泛研究，但将其应用于量子系统需处理通过未知动态演化的隐藏量子态。我们通过一个框架形式化该问题：环境通过未知量子信道演化隐藏的量子记忆，智能体使用量子仪器顺序干预。针对此场景，我们改进了一种乐观最大似然估计算法，并将分析扩展至连续动作空间，从而能够建模一般正算子值测度（POVM）。通过控制估计误差在量子信道和仪器中的传播，我们证明该策略在K个回合中的累积遗憾按$\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(\sqrt{K})$缩放。此外，通过归约至多臂量子赌博机问题，我们建立了信息论下界，证明该次线性缩放在多对数因子内严格最优。作为物理应用，我们考虑状态无关的功提取问题：当从由隐藏记忆关联的非独立同分布量子态序列中提取自由能时，对信源知识的任何缺失都会导致热力学耗散。在我们的框架中，数学遗憾精确量化了这种累积耗散。通过自适应算法，智能体利用过往能量结果实时改进提取协议，实现次线性累积耗散，从而达成渐近零耗散率。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of applying reinforcement learning to quantum systems with memory, where an agent must explore and exploit unknown quantum dynamics to maximize a reward, a problem complicated by hidden quantum states and non-i.i.d. correlations. The authors formalize this as a sequential interaction problem with a quantum memory evolving via unknown channels, adapt an optimistic maximum-likelihood estimation algorithm to handle continuous action spaces like general POVMs, and rigorously control estimation errors. Their main result proves that the cumulative regret scales optimally as Õ(√K) over K episodes, with information-theoretic lower bounds confirming this sublinear scaling is near-optimal. As a key application, they show this regret directly quantifies thermodynamic dissipation in state-agnostic work extraction from correlated quantum states, and their adaptive algorithm achieves sublinear cumulative dissipation, leading to an asymptotically zero dissipation rate.
本文研究了强化学习在具有记忆的量子系统中的应用挑战，其中智能体必须探索和利用未知的量子动力学以最大化奖励，这一问题因隐藏的量子态和非独立同分布的相关性而变得复杂。作者将其形式化为一个与通过未知信道演化的量子内存进行顺序交互的问题，采用了一种乐观的最大似然估计算法来处理连续动作空间（如广义POVM），并严格控制了估计误差。主要结果证明，在K个回合中，累积遗憾的最优缩放为Õ(√K)，且信息论下界证实了这种次线性缩放近乎最优。作为一个关键应用，他们表明这种遗憾直接量化了从相关量子态中进行状态无关功提取时的热力学耗散，并且他们的自适应算法实现了次线性累积耗散，从而使得耗散率渐近趋于零。
