First: 2026-03-26T05:21:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T05:21:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce Intern-S1-Pro, the first one-trillion-parameter scientific multimodal foundation model. Scaling to this unprecedented size, the model delivers a comprehensive enhancement across both general and scientific domains. Beyond stronger reasoning and image-text understanding capabilities, its intelligence is augmented with advanced agent capabilities. Simultaneously, its scientific expertise has been vastly expanded to master over 100 specialized tasks across critical science fields, including chemistry, materials, life sciences, and earth sciences. Achieving this massive scale is made possible by the robust infrastructure support of XTuner and LMDeploy, which facilitates highly efficient Reinforcement Learning (RL) training at the 1-trillion parameter level while ensuring strict precision consistency between training and inference. By seamlessly integrating these advancements, Intern-S1-Pro further fortifies the fusion of general and specialized intelligence, working as a Specializable Generalist, demonstrating its position in the top tier of open-source models for general capabilities, while outperforming proprietary models in the depth of specialized scientific tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Intern-S1-Pro：万亿参数科学多模态基础模型
我们推出首个万亿参数科学多模态基础模型Intern-S1-Pro。该模型通过扩展至前所未有的规模，在通用领域与科学领域均实现全面增强。除具备更强的推理与图文理解能力外，其智能体通过高级代理能力得到强化。同时，其科学专业知识大幅扩展，可覆盖化学、材料、生命科学、地球科学等关键科学领域的百余项专项任务。实现此大规模扩展得益于XTuner与LMDeploy提供的坚实基础设施支持，二者保障了万亿参数级别的高效强化学习训练，并确保训练与推理间的严格精度一致性。通过无缝整合这些进展，Intern-S1-Pro进一步强化通用智能与专业智能的融合，作为‘可专业化通才’，在通用能力方面跻身开源模型前列，并在专业科学任务的深度上超越闭源模型。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind Intern-S1-Pro is to create a scientific multimodal foundation model at an unprecedented trillion-parameter scale to enhance both general and specialized scientific intelligence. The method involves scaling the model to one trillion parameters, supported by the XTuner and LMDeploy infrastructure for efficient reinforcement learning training while maintaining precision consistency between training and inference. The main experimental results show that the model delivers comprehensive enhancements in reasoning and image-text understanding, augments intelligence with advanced agent capabilities, and masters over 100 specialized scientific tasks across fields like chemistry and life sciences, outperforming proprietary models in specialized task depth while ranking among top open-source models in general capabilities.
Intern-S1-Pro的研发动机是构建一个前所未有的万亿参数规模科学多模态基础模型，以增强通用和专业化科学智能。方法上，模型扩展至万亿参数，并依托XTuner和LMDeploy基础设施实现高效的强化学习训练，同时确保训练与推理间的精度一致性。主要实验结果表明，该模型在推理和图文理解方面实现全面增强，具备先进的智能体能力，并精通化学、生命科学等关键领域的100多项专业科学任务，在专业任务深度上超越闭源模型，同时在通用能力上跻身顶级开源模型之列。
Revealing Human Attention Patterns from Gameplay Analysis for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Henrik Krauss, Takehisa Yairi
First: 2025-04-15T12:07:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T04:03:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This study introduces a novel method for revealing human internal attention patterns (decision-relevant attention) from gameplay data alone, leveraging offline attention techniques from reinforcement learning (RL). We propose contextualized, task-relevant (CTR) attention networks, which generate attention maps from both human and RL agent gameplay in Atari environments. To evaluate whether the human CTR maps reveal internal attention patterns, we validate our model by quantitative and qualitative comparison to the agent maps as well as to a temporally integrated overt attention (TIOA) model based on human eye-tracking data. Our results show that human CTR maps are more sparse than the agent ones and align better with the TIOA maps. Following a qualitative visual comparison we conclude that they likely capture patterns of internal attention. As a further application, we use these maps to guide RL agents, finding that human attention-guided agents achieve slightly improved and more stable learning compared to baselines, and significantly outperform TIOA-based agents. This work advances the understanding of human-agent attention differences and provides a new approach for extracting and validating internal attention patterns from behavioral data.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于游戏分析揭示人类注意力模式以用于强化学习
本研究提出一种新方法，仅通过游戏数据揭示人类内部注意力模式（决策相关注意力），利用强化学习中的离线注意力技术。我们提出情境化任务相关注意力网络，该网络可从人类和强化学习智能体在Atari环境中的游戏生成注意力图。为评估人类情境化任务相关注意力图是否揭示内部注意力模式，我们通过定量和定性比较智能体注意力图以及基于人类眼动数据的时序整合显性注意力模型来验证模型。结果显示，人类情境化任务相关注意力图比智能体图更稀疏，且与时序整合显性注意力图更一致。经定性视觉比较，我们推断其可能捕捉到内部注意力模式。作为进一步应用，我们使用这些图指导强化学习智能体，发现人类注意力引导的智能体相比基线实现轻微改进且学习更稳定，并显著优于基于时序整合显性注意力的智能体。该工作推进了对人类与智能体注意力差异的理解，并为从行为数据提取和验证内部注意力模式提供了新方法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to understand human internal attention patterns from behavioral data without direct physiological measurement, this study proposes contextualized, task-relevant (CTR) attention networks to generate attention maps from gameplay in Atari environments. The method leverages offline reinforcement learning techniques to derive these maps from both human and RL agent gameplay, then validates them through quantitative and qualitative comparisons against agent-generated maps and a temporally integrated overt attention model based on human eye-tracking data. Experimental results show that human CTR maps are sparser than agent maps and align better with the overt attention model, suggesting they capture internal attention patterns; additionally, using these maps to guide RL agents leads to slightly improved, more stable learning compared to baselines and significantly outperforms agents guided by overt attention.
本研究旨在从行为数据中揭示人类内部注意力模式，而无需直接生理测量，为此提出了情境化任务相关注意力网络，用于从Atari游戏环境中的人类和强化学习智能体游戏数据生成注意力图。该方法利用离线强化学习技术，从游戏数据中推导注意力图，并通过与智能体生成图以及基于人类眼动数据的时序整合显性注意力模型进行定量和定性比较来验证。实验结果表明，人类注意力图比智能体图更稀疏，且与显性注意力模型更一致，表明其捕捉了内部注意力模式；此外，使用这些图指导强化学习智能体能带来比基线稍好且更稳定的学习效果，并显著优于基于显性注意力的智能体。
Learning Rollout from Sampling:An R1-Style Tokenized Traffic Simulation Model
Authors: Ziyan Wang, Peng Chen, Ding Li, Chiwei Li, Qichao Zhang, Zhongpu Xia, Guizhen Yu
First: 2026-03-26T03:29:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T03:29:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Learning diverse and high-fidelity traffic simulations from human driving demonstrations is crucial for autonomous driving evaluation. The recent next-token prediction (NTP) paradigm, widely adopted in large language models (LLMs), has been applied to traffic simulation and achieves iterative improvements via supervised fine-tuning (SFT). However, such methods limit active exploration of potentially valuable motion tokens, particularly in suboptimal regions. Entropy patterns provide a promising perspective for enabling exploration driven by motion token uncertainty. Motivated by this insight, we propose a novel tokenized traffic simulation policy, R1Sim, which represents an initial attempt to explore reinforcement learning based on motion token entropy patterns, and systematically analyzes the impact of different motion tokens on simulation outcomes. Specifically, we introduce an entropy-guided adaptive sampling mechanism that focuses on previously overlooked motion tokens with high uncertainty yet high potential. We further optimize motion behaviors using Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), guided by a safety-aware reward design. Overall, these components enable a balanced exploration-exploitation trade-off through diverse high-uncertainty sampling and group-wise comparative estimation, resulting in realistic, safe, and diverse multi-agent behaviors. Extensive experiments on the Waymo Sim Agent benchmark demonstrate that R1Sim achieves competitive performance compared to state-of-the-art methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于采样的学习推演：一种R1风格的分词化交通仿真模型
从人类驾驶示范中学习多样且高保真的交通仿真对自动驾驶评估至关重要。近期广泛应用于大语言模型（LLM）的下一个词元预测（NTP）范式已被应用于交通仿真，并通过监督微调（SFT）实现迭代改进。然而，此类方法限制了潜在价值运动词元的主动探索，尤其在次优区域。熵模式为基于运动词元不确定性的探索提供了可行视角。受此启发，我们提出一种新颖的分词化交通仿真策略R1Sim，这是首次尝试基于运动词元熵模式探索强化学习，并系统分析不同运动词元对仿真结果的影响。具体而言，我们引入熵引导的自适应采样机制，重点关注先前被忽视的具有高不确定性与高潜力的运动词元。在安全感知奖励设计的指导下，我们进一步采用组相对策略优化（GRPO）优化运动行为。整体上，这些组件通过多样化高不确定性采样和组间对比估计，实现了探索与利用的平衡权衡，从而生成真实、安全且多样的多智能体行为。在Waymo Sim Agent基准上的大量实验表明，R1Sim相比现有先进方法具有竞争优势。
Summary / 总结
The motivation is to enhance autonomous driving evaluation by learning diverse and high-fidelity traffic simulations from human demonstrations, addressing limitations in next-token prediction methods that restrict exploration in suboptimal regions. The method introduces R1Sim, a tokenized traffic simulation policy that leverages entropy patterns to guide exploration, featuring an entropy-guided adaptive sampling mechanism to focus on high-uncertainty motion tokens and optimizing behaviors with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) under safety-aware rewards. Main experimental results on the Waymo Sim Agent benchmark show that R1Sim achieves competitive performance, producing realistic, safe, and diverse multi-agent behaviors through balanced exploration-exploitation.
该研究的动机是通过从人类驾驶演示中学习多样且高保真的交通仿真来提升自动驾驶评估，针对现有基于下一令牌预测的方法在次优区域探索受限的问题。方法上提出了R1Sim，一种基于运动令牌熵模式的强化学习仿真策略，采用熵引导的自适应采样机制关注高不确定性令牌，并结合安全感知奖励设计，通过组相对策略优化（GRPO）来优化行为。在Waymo Sim Agent基准上的大量实验结果表明，R1Sim实现了与先进方法竞争的性能，能生成真实、安全且多样的多智能体行为。
Composer 2 Technical Report
Authors: Cursor Research, :, Aaron Chan, Ahmed Shalaby, Alexander Wettig, Aman Sanger, Andrew Zhai, Anurag Ajay, Ashvin Nair, Charlie Snell, Chen Lu, Chen Shen, Emily Jia, Federico Cassano, Hanpeng Liu, Haoyu Chen, Henry Wildermuth, Jacob Jackson, Janet Li, Jediah Katz, Jiajun Yao, Joey Hejna, Josh Warner, Julius Vering, Kevin Frans, Lee Danilek, Less Wright, Lujing Cen, Luke Melas-Kyriazi, Michael Truell, Michiel de Jong, Naman Jain, Nate Schmidt, Nathan Wang, Niklas Muennighoff, Oleg Rybkin, Paul Loh, Phillip Kravtsov, Rishabh Yadav, Sahil Shah, Sam Kottler, Alexander M Rush, Shengtong Zhang, Shomil Jain, Sriram Sankar, Stefan Heule, Stuart H. Sul, Sualeh Asif, Victor Rong, Wanqi Zhu, William Lin, Yuchen Wu, Yuri Volkov, Yury Zemlyanskiy, Zack Holbrook, Zhiyuan Zhang
First: 2026-03-25T16:18:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T01:57:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Composer 2 is a specialized model designed for agentic software engineering. The model demonstrates strong long-term planning and coding intelligence while maintaining the ability to efficiently solve problems for interactive use. The model is trained in two phases: first, continued pretraining to improve the model's knowledge and latent coding ability, followed by large-scale reinforcement learning to improve end-to-end coding performance through stronger reasoning, accurate multi-step execution, and coherence on long-horizon realistic coding problems. We develop infrastructure to support training in the same Cursor harness that is used by the deployed model, with equivalent tools and structure, and use environments that match real problems closely. To measure the ability of the model on increasingly difficult tasks, we introduce a benchmark derived from real software engineering problems in large codebases including our own. Composer 2 is a frontier-level coding model and demonstrates a process for training strong domain-specialized models. On our CursorBench evaluations the model achieves a major improvement in accuracy compared to previous Composer models (61.3). On public benchmarks the model scores 61.7 on Terminal-Bench and 73.7 on SWE-bench Multilingual in our harness, comparable to state-of-the-art systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Composer 2技术报告
Composer 2是一款专为智能体软件工程设计的专业模型。该模型展现出强大的长期规划与编码智能，同时保持高效解决交互使用问题的能力。模型训练分为两个阶段：首先通过持续预训练提升模型知识与潜在编码能力，随后进行大规模强化学习，通过增强推理能力、精准多步骤执行以及对长周期现实编码问题的连贯性，提升端到端编码性能。我们开发了与部署模型所用Cursor框架相匹配的基础设施，配备同等工具与结构，并采用高度贴近实际问题的训练环境。为衡量模型在逐级复杂任务上的能力，我们引入了基于大型代码库（包括自有代码库）中真实软件工程问题的基准测试。Composer 2是前沿级编码模型，展示了训练强领域专业化模型的完整流程。在CursorBench评估中，该模型相比前代Composer模型（61.3分）实现显著精度提升；在公开基准测试中，模型在我们的测试框架下取得Terminal-Bench 61.7分、SWE-bench Multilingual 73.7分的成绩，达到业界领先系统水平。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for advanced agentic software engineering models capable of long-term planning and interactive problem-solving, this paper introduces Composer 2, a specialized model trained in two phases: continued pretraining to enhance coding knowledge, followed by large-scale reinforcement learning to improve reasoning and execution on realistic, long-horizon coding tasks. The method leverages infrastructure that mirrors the deployment environment, using tools and structures from the Cursor harness and environments closely matching real problems. Experimental results show Composer 2 achieves a major accuracy improvement on the internal CursorBench (61.3) and performs comparably to state-of-the-art systems on public benchmarks, scoring 61.7 on Terminal-Bench and 73.7 on SWE-bench Multilingual.
本研究旨在开发具备长期规划和交互式问题解决能力的高级智能软件工程模型，为此提出了Composer 2。该方法采用两阶段训练：首先通过持续预训练增强模型的编程知识，然后通过大规模强化学习提升其在真实、长周期编码任务中的推理与执行能力，并利用与部署环境一致的Cursor工具框架和贴近实际问题的环境进行训练。实验结果表明，Composer 2在内部CursorBench上实现了显著精度提升（61.3），在公开基准测试中表现与前沿系统相当，在Terminal-Bench和SWE-bench Multilingual上分别获得61.7和73.7的分数。
When Should a Robot Think? Resource-Aware Reasoning via Reinforcement Learning for Embodied Robotic Decision-Making
Authors: Jun Liu, Pu Zhao, Zhenglun Kong, Xuan Shen, Peiyan Dong, Fan Yang, Lin Cui, Hao Tang, Geng Yuan, Wei Niu, Wenbin Zhang, Xue Lin, Gaowen Liu, Yanzhi Wang, Dong Huang
First: 2026-03-17T15:38:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T01:08:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Embodied robotic systems increasingly rely on large language model (LLM)-based agents to support high-level reasoning, planning, and decision-making during interactions with the environment. However, invoking LLM reasoning introduces substantial computational latency and resource overhead, which can interrupt action execution and reduce system reliability. Excessive reasoning may delay actions, while insufficient reasoning often leads to incorrect decisions and task failures. This raises a fundamental question for embodied agents: when should the agent reason, and when should it act? In this work, we propose RARRL (Resource-Aware Reasoning via Reinforcement Learning), a hierarchical framework for resource-aware orchestration of embodied agents. Rather than learning low-level control policies, RARRL learns a high-level orchestration policy that operates at the agent's decision-making layer. This policy enables the agent to adaptively determine whether to invoke reasoning, which reasoning role to employ, and how much computational budget to allocate based on current observations, execution history, and remaining resources. Extensive experiments, including evaluations with empirical latency profiles derived from the ALFRED benchmark, show that RARRL consistently improves task success rates while reducing execution latency and enhancing robustness compared with fixed or heuristic reasoning strategies. These results demonstrate that adaptive reasoning control is essential for building reliable and efficient embodied robotic agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：机器人何时应思考？基于强化学习的资源感知推理在具身机器人决策中的应用
具身机器人系统日益依赖基于大语言模型（LLM）的智能体，以支持其在与环境交互过程中的高层推理、规划与决策。然而，调用LLM推理会带来显著的计算延迟与资源开销，可能中断动作执行并降低系统可靠性。过度推理会延迟行动，而推理不足则常导致错误决策与任务失败。这引发了一个具身智能体的根本性问题：智能体应在何时推理，又在何时行动？本研究提出RARRL（基于强化学习的资源感知推理），一种用于具身智能体资源感知编排的分层框架。RARRL并非学习底层控制策略，而是学习在智能体决策层运作的高层编排策略。该策略使智能体能够根据当前观察、执行历史与剩余资源，自适应地决定是否调用推理、采用何种推理角色以及分配多少计算预算。大量实验（包括基于ALFRED基准衍生的实际延迟配置文件评估）表明，相较于固定或启发式推理策略，RARRL在持续提升任务成功率的同时，有效降低了执行延迟并增强了系统鲁棒性。这些结果证明，自适应推理控制对于构建可靠高效的具身机器人智能体至关重要。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of balancing computational resource use with decision-making quality in embodied robotic systems that employ large language models (LLMs) for reasoning, where excessive reasoning causes latency and insufficient reasoning leads to errors. The authors propose RARRL, a hierarchical reinforcement learning framework that learns a high-level orchestration policy to adaptively decide when to invoke reasoning, which reasoning role to use, and how much computational budget to allocate based on observations, history, and resources. Experimental evaluations using latency profiles from the ALFRED benchmark demonstrate that RARRL improves task success rates, reduces execution latency, and enhances robustness compared to fixed or heuristic reasoning strategies, highlighting the importance of adaptive reasoning control for efficient and reliable robotic agents.
本文针对具身机器人系统使用大语言模型进行推理时面临的挑战，即过度推理会导致延迟，而推理不足则引发决策错误，旨在平衡计算资源与决策质量。作者提出了RARRL，一种基于分层强化学习的框架，通过学习高层编排策略，使机器人能根据当前观察、执行历史和剩余资源自适应地决定何时调用推理、使用何种推理角色以及分配多少计算预算。基于ALFRED基准的延迟配置文件进行的实验评估表明，与固定或启发式推理策略相比，RARRL能提高任务成功率、降低执行延迟并增强系统鲁棒性，这证明了自适应推理控制对于构建高效可靠具身机器人的重要性。
Integrated Multi-Drone Task Allocation, Sequencing, and Optimal Trajectory Generation in Obstacle-Rich 3D Environments
Authors: Yunes Alqudsi, Murat Makaraci
First: 2026-03-26T00:46:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-26T00:46:26+00:00
Comments: Resubmission following accepted appeal (MOD-78958). Resubmitting to cs.RO with cross-lists cs.MA and cs.AI as advised by arXiv Support
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Coordinating teams of aerial robots in cluttered three-dimensional (3D) environments requires a principled integration of discrete mission planning-deciding which robot serves which goals and in what order -- with continuous-time trajectory synthesis that enforces collision avoidance and dynamic feasibility. This paper introduces IMD-TAPP (Integrated Multi-Drone Task Allocation and Path Planning), an end-to-end framework that jointly addresses multi-goal allocation, tour sequencing, and safe trajectory generation for quadrotor teams operating in obstacle-rich spaces. IMD--TAPP first discretizes the workspace into a 3D navigation graph and computes obstacle-aware robot-to-goal and goal-to-goal travel costs via graph-search-based pathfinding. These costs are then embedded within an Injected Particle Swarm Optimization (IPSO) scheme, guided by multiple linear assignment, to efficiently explore coupled assignment/ordering alternatives and to minimize mission makespan. Finally, the resulting waypoint tours are transformed into time-parameterized minimum-snap trajectories through a generation-and-optimization routine equipped with iterative validation of obstacle clearance and inter-robot separation, triggering re-planning when safety margins are violated. Extensive MATLAB simulations across cluttered 3D scenarios demonstrate that IMD--TAPP consistently produces dynamically feasible, collision-free trajectories while achieving competitive completion times. In a representative case study with two drones serving multiple goals, the proposed approach attains a minimum mission time of 136~s while maintaining the required safety constraints throughout execution.
中文标题/摘要
标题：障碍密集三维环境中多无人机任务分配、序列化与最优轨迹生成的集成方法
在杂乱三维环境中协调空中机器人团队，需要将离散任务规划（决定各机器人服务的目标点及顺序）与连续时间轨迹合成（确保避碰和动态可行性）进行系统性整合。本文提出IMD-TAPP（集成多无人机任务分配与路径规划）框架，该端到端方案可协同处理障碍密集空间中四旋翼机群的多目标分配、巡回序列规划及安全轨迹生成。IMD-TAPP首先将工作空间离散化为三维导航图，通过基于图搜索的路径规划计算机器人-目标间及目标-目标间的障碍感知移动成本。随后将这些成本嵌入注入式粒子群优化算法，并以多重线性分配为引导，高效探索任务分配与顺序的耦合解空间，以最小化任务完成时间。最终通过配备障碍间隙与机间距离迭代验证的生成-优化流程，将生成的航点巡回序列转化为时间参数化的最小加加速度轨迹，并在安全裕度被违反时触发重规划。在多种杂乱三维场景下的MATLAB仿真表明，IMD-TAPP能持续生成动态可行、无碰撞的轨迹，同时获得具有竞争力的任务完成时间。在双无人机服务多目标的典型案例中，该方法在全程保持安全约束的前提下实现了136秒的最短任务时间。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of coordinating drone teams in cluttered 3D environments by integrating discrete task planning with continuous trajectory generation. The proposed IMD-TAPP framework first constructs a 3D navigation graph to compute obstacle-aware travel costs, then uses an Injected Particle Swarm Optimization scheme guided by linear assignment to jointly optimize task allocation and sequencing for minimizing mission makespan. Finally, it generates time-parameterized minimum-snap trajectories with iterative safety validation. Experimental simulations in MATLAB demonstrate that the method produces dynamically feasible, collision-free trajectories, achieving a mission time of 136 seconds in a case study with two drones while maintaining all safety constraints.
本文针对杂乱三维环境中无人机团队的协调问题，提出了将离散任务规划与连续轨迹生成相集成的解决方案。所提出的IMD-TAPP框架首先构建三维导航图以计算障碍物感知的旅行成本，然后利用由线性分配引导的注入粒子群优化方案，联合优化任务分配与排序以最小化任务完成时间。最后，通过带有迭代安全验证的生成优化例程，生成时间参数化的最小加加速度轨迹。在MATLAB中的大量仿真实验表明，该方法能产生动态可行且无碰撞的轨迹，在一个双无人机案例中实现了136秒的任务时间，同时全程保持了所需的安全约束。
Learning to Staff: Offline Reinforcement Learning and Fine-Tuned LLMs for Warehouse Staffing Optimization
Authors: Kalle Kujanpää, Yuying Zhu, Kristina Klinkner, Shervin Malmasi
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-25T23:56:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T23:56:25+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026 Workshop on AI for Mechanism Design and Strategic Decision Making
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We investigate machine learning approaches for optimizing real-time staffing decisions in semi-automated warehouse sortation systems. Operational decision-making can be supported at different levels of abstraction, with different trade-offs. We evaluate two approaches, each in a matching simulation environment. First, we train custom Transformer-based policies using offline reinforcement learning on detailed historical state representations, achieving a 2.4% throughput improvement over historical baselines in learned simulators. In high-volume warehouse operations, improvements of this size translate to significant savings. Second, we explore LLMs operating on abstracted, human-readable state descriptions. These are a natural fit for decisions that warehouse managers make using high-level operational summaries. We systematically compare prompting techniques, automatic prompt optimization, and fine-tuning strategies. While prompting alone proves insufficient, supervised fine-tuning combined with Direct Preference Optimization on simulator-generated preferences achieves performance that matches or slightly exceeds historical baselines in a hand-crafted simulator. Our findings demonstrate that both approaches offer viable paths toward AI-assisted operational decision-making. Offline RL excels with task-specific architectures. LLMs support human-readable inputs and can be combined with an iterative feedback loop that can incorporate manager preferences.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习人员配置：基于离线强化学习与微调大语言模型的仓库人员配置优化
本研究探讨机器学习在半自动化仓库分拣系统中优化实时人员配置决策的方法。运营决策支持可在不同抽象层级实现，各有权衡。我们在匹配的仿真环境中评估两种方法：首先，基于详细历史状态表征，采用离线强化学习训练定制化Transformer策略，在习得模拟器中实现较历史基线2.4%的吞吐量提升，这在大型仓库运营中意味着显著成本节约；其次，探索大语言模型处理抽象化、人类可读状态描述的能力，该方法天然契合仓库管理者基于高层运营摘要的决策场景。我们系统比较了提示技术、自动提示优化与微调策略：单纯提示法效果有限，但监督微调结合模拟器生成偏好的直接偏好优化，在手工构建模拟器中达到或略超历史基线的性能。研究表明两种方法均为AI辅助运营决策提供可行路径：离线强化学习在任务专用架构中表现卓越，大语言模型支持人类可读输入，并能与融入管理者偏好的迭代反馈循环相结合。

Gaze patterns predict preference and confidence in pairwise AI image evaluation
Authors: Nikolas Papadopoulos, Shreenithi Navaneethan, Sheng Bai, Ankur Samanta, Paul Sajda
First: 2026-03-25T22:30:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T22:30:40+00:00
Comments: This paper has been accepted to ACM ETRA 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Preference learning methods, such as Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) and Direct Preference Optimization (DPO), rely on pairwise human judgments, yet little is known about the cognitive processes underlying these judgments. We investigate whether eye-tracking can reveal preference formation during pairwise AI-generated image evaluation. Thirty participants completed 1,800 trials while their gaze was recorded. We replicated the gaze cascade effect, with gaze shifting toward chosen images approximately one second before the decision. Cascade dynamics were consistent across confidence levels. Gaze features predicted binary choice (68% accuracy), with chosen images receiving more dwell time, fixations, and revisits. Gaze transitions distinguished high-confidence from uncertain decisions (66% accuracy), with low-confidence trials showing more image switches per second. These results show that gaze patterns predict both choice and confidence in pairwise image evaluations, suggesting that eye-tracking provides implicit signals relevant to the quality of preference annotations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：注视模式可预测成对AI图像评估中的偏好与置信度
基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）和直接偏好优化（DPO）等偏好学习方法依赖于成对人类判断，但这些判断背后的认知过程尚不明确。本研究通过眼动追踪探究成对AI生成图像评估中的偏好形成机制。30名参与者在完成1800次试验时被记录注视数据。我们复现了注视级联效应：决策前约一秒，注视会向被选图像转移。级联动态在不同置信度水平间保持一致。注视特征可预测二元选择（准确率68%），被选图像获得更长的停留时间、更多注视点和回视。注视转移模式能区分高置信度与不确定决策（准确率66%），低置信度试验中每秒图像切换更频繁。结果表明注视模式可同时预测成对图像评估中的选择和置信度，说明眼动追踪能提供与偏好标注质量相关的隐性信号。

Reaching Beyond the Mode: RL for Distributional Reasoning in Language Models
Authors: Isha Puri, Mehul Damani, Idan Shenfeld, Marzyeh Ghassemi, Jacob Andreas, Yoon Kim
First: 2026-03-25T22:20:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T22:20:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Given a question, a language model (LM) implicitly encodes a distribution over possible answers. In practice, post-training procedures for LMs often collapse this distribution onto a single dominant mode. While this is generally not a problem for benchmark-style evaluations that assume one correct answer, many real-world tasks inherently involve multiple valid answers or irreducible uncertainty. Examples include medical diagnosis, ambiguous question answering, and settings with incomplete information. In these cases, we would like LMs to generate multiple plausible hypotheses, ideally with confidence estimates for each one, and without computationally intensive repeated sampling to generate non-modal answers. This paper describes a multi-answer reinforcement learning approach for training LMs to perform distributional reasoning over multiple answers during inference. We modify the RL objective to enable models to explicitly generate multiple candidate answers in a single forward pass, internalizing aspects of inference-time search into the model's generative process. Across question-answering, medical diagnostic, and coding benchmarks, we observe improved diversity, coverage, and set-level calibration scores compared to single answer trained baselines. Models trained with our approach require fewer tokens to generate multiple answers than competing approaches. On coding tasks, they are also substantially more accurate. These results position multi-answer RL as a principled and compute-efficient alternative to inference-time scaling procedures such as best-of-k. Code and more information can be found at https://multi-answer-rl.github.io/.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越单一模式：语言模型中的分布推理强化学习方法
给定一个问题，语言模型（LM）隐式编码了可能答案的分布。实践中，LM的后训练过程常将该分布坍缩至单一主导模式。虽然这对假设单一正确答案的基准评估通常无碍，但许多现实任务天然涉及多个有效答案或不可约的不确定性，例如医疗诊断、模糊问答和信息不完整场景。在这些情况下，我们希望LM能生成多个合理假设，最好附带各假设的置信度估计，且无需依赖计算密集的重复采样来生成非模态答案。本文提出一种多答案强化学习方法，用于训练LM在推理时对多个答案进行分布推理。我们修改强化学习目标，使模型能在单次前向传播中显式生成多个候选答案，将推理时搜索的部分机制内化至模型生成过程。在问答、医疗诊断和代码生成基准测试中，相较于单答案训练基线，该方法在多样性、覆盖率和集合级校准分数上均有提升。使用本方法训练的模型生成多个答案所需标记数少于对比方法，在代码任务中准确性也显著更高。这些结果表明多答案强化学习可作为推理时扩展方法（如k优采样）的一种原则性且计算高效的替代方案。代码与更多信息详见 https://multi-answer-rl.github.io/。

The paper is motivated by the observation that standard post-training procedures for language models collapse their inherent answer distributions onto a single mode, which is insufficient for real-world tasks like medical diagnosis or ambiguous QA that involve multiple valid answers or uncertainty. Experimental results across question-answering, medical diagnostic, and coding benchmarks show that this approach improves answer diversity, coverage, and set-level calibration, requires fewer tokens to generate multiple answers than alternatives, and achieves substantially higher accuracy on coding tasks, positioning it as a compute-efficient alternative to methods like best-of-k sampling.

Ludax: A GPU-Accelerated Domain Specific Language for Board Games
Authors: Graham Todd, Alexander G. Padula, Dennis J. N. J. Soemers, Julian Togelius
First: 2025-06-27T20:15:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T21:12:45+00:00
Comments: 25 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Games have long been used as benchmarks and testing environments for research in artificial intelligence. A key step in supporting this research was the development of game description languages: frameworks that compile domain-specific code into playable and simulatable game environments, allowing researchers to generalize their algorithms and approaches across multiple games without having to manually implement each one. More recently, progress in reinforcement learning (RL) has been largely driven by advances in hardware acceleration. Libraries like JAX allow practitioners to take full advantage of cutting-edge computing hardware, often speeding up training and testing by orders of magnitude. Here, we present a synthesis of these strands of research: a domain-specific language for board games which automatically compiles into hardware-accelerated code. Our framework, Ludax, combines the generality of game description languages with the speed of modern parallel processing hardware and is designed to fit neatly into existing deep learning pipelines. We envision Ludax as a tool to help accelerate games research generally, from RL to cognitive science, by enabling rapid simulation and providing a flexible representation scheme. We present a detailed breakdown of Ludax's description language and technical notes on the compilation process, along with speed benchmarking and a demonstration of training RL agents. The Ludax framework, along with implementations of existing board games, is open-source and freely available.

标题：Ludax：一种面向棋盘游戏的GPU加速领域特定语言
游戏长期以来被用作人工智能研究的基准和测试环境。支持此类研究的关键一步是游戏描述语言的开发：这类框架将领域特定代码编译为可玩且可模拟的游戏环境，使研究者能够跨多种游戏泛化其算法与方法，无需手动逐一实现。近年来，强化学习（RL）的进展主要受硬件加速技术推动。JAX等库让从业者能充分利用尖端计算硬件，常将训练与测试速度提升数个数量级。本文融合了这两类研究方向：提出一种面向棋盘游戏的领域特定语言，可自动编译为硬件加速代码。我们的框架Ludax结合了游戏描述语言的通用性与现代并行处理硬件的速度，并设计为能无缝集成至现有深度学习流程中。我们设想Ludax将成为加速游戏研究的通用工具——从强化学习到认知科学——通过支持快速模拟并提供灵活的表征方案。本文详细解析了Ludax的描述语言及编译过程的技术说明，同时提供了速度基准测试与强化学习智能体训练示例。Ludax框架及现有棋盘游戏的实现均已开源并免费提供。

Trust as Monitoring: Evolutionary Dynamics of User Trust and AI Developer Behaviour
Authors: Adeela Bashir, Zhao Song, Ndidi Bianca Ogbo, Nataliya Balabanova, Martin Smit, Chin-wing Leung, Paolo Bova, Manuel Chica Serrano, Dhanushka Dissanayake, Manh Hong Duong, Elias Fernandez Domingos, Nikita Huber-Kralj, Marcus Krellner, Andrew Powell, Stefan Sarkadi, Fernando P. Santos, Zia Ush Shamszaman, Chaimaa Tarzi, Paolo Turrini, Grace Ibukunoluwa Ufeoshi, Victor A. Vargas-Perez, Alessandro Di Stefano, Simon T. Powers, The Anh Han
First: 2026-03-25T19:04:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T19:04:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
AI safety is an increasingly urgent concern as the capabilities and adoption of AI systems grow. Existing evolutionary models of AI governance have primarily examined incentives for safe development and effective regulation, typically representing users' trust as a one-shot adoption choice rather than as a dynamic, evolving process shaped by repeated interactions. We instead model trust as reduced monitoring in a repeated, asymmetric interaction between users and AI developers, where checking AI behaviour is costly. Using evolutionary game theory, we study how user trust strategies and developer choices between safe (compliant) and unsafe (non-compliant) AI co-evolve under different levels of monitoring cost and institutional regimes. We complement the infinite-population replicator analysis with stochastic finite-population dynamics and reinforcement learning (Q-learning) simulations. Across these approaches, we find three robust long-run regimes: no adoption with unsafe development, unsafe but widely adopted systems, and safe systems that are widely adopted. Only the last is desirable, and it arises when penalties for unsafe behaviour exceed the extra cost of safety and users can still afford to monitor at least occasionally. Our results formally support governance proposals that emphasise transparency, low-cost monitoring, and meaningful sanctions, and they show that neither regulation alone nor blind user trust is sufficient to prevent evolutionary drift towards unsafe or low-adoption outcomes.
中文标题/摘要
标题：信任即监督：用户信任与AI开发者行为的演化动力学
随着AI系统能力与应用范围的扩大，AI安全性日益成为紧迫议题。现有AI治理演化模型主要关注安全开发与有效监管的激励机制，通常将用户信任视为一次性采纳选择，而非由重复互动塑造的动态演化过程。本研究将信任建模为用户与AI开发者之间重复非对称互动中的监督弱化，其中检查AI行为需付出成本。运用演化博弈论，我们探究在不同监督成本与制度环境下，用户信任策略与开发者在安全（合规）和不安全（违规）AI之间的选择如何协同演化。除无限群体复制者动态分析外，还结合随机有限群体动力学与强化学习（Q学习）模拟进行补充。所有方法均揭示出三种稳健的长期演化机制：不安全开发且无采纳、不安全但广泛采纳的系统、以及安全且广泛采纳的系统。仅最后一种为理想状态，其形成条件是不安全行为的惩罚超过安全额外成本，且用户仍能承担至少偶尔的监督成本。研究结果从形式上支持强调透明度、低成本监督与有效制裁的治理方案，并表明仅靠监管或盲目的用户信任均不足以阻止系统向不安全或低采纳状态的演化漂移。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to understand AI safety governance beyond static models, this paper reconceptualizes user trust as a dynamic reduction in costly monitoring within repeated user-developer interactions. The method employs evolutionary game theory, analyzing infinite-population replicator dynamics alongside stochastic finite-population simulations and Q-learning to model the co-evolution of user monitoring strategies and developer choices between safe and unsafe AI. The main experimental results identify three robust long-term regimes: no adoption with unsafe development, widespread adoption of unsafe systems, and the desirable outcome of widespread adoption of safe systems, which emerges only when penalties for unsafe behavior outweigh safety costs and users retain affordable monitoring options, thereby underscoring the necessity of transparency, low-cost monitoring, and effective sanctions over mere regulation or blind trust.
本文的动机是超越静态模型，以理解AI安全治理，将用户信任重新定义为在重复的用户与开发者互动中，对成本高昂的监控行为的动态减少。研究方法采用演化博弈论，结合无限种群的复制者动态分析、随机有限种群模拟以及Q学习，来模拟用户监控策略与开发者在安全和不安全AI之间选择的共同演化。主要实验结果揭示了三种稳健的长期状态：不安全开发且无采用、不安全系统被广泛采用，以及理想的安全系统被广泛采用；只有当对不安全行为的惩罚超过安全成本且用户仍能负担偶尔的监控时，最后一种理想状态才会出现，这强调了透明度、低成本监控和有效制裁的必要性，而非仅仅依靠监管或盲目的用户信任。
Decentralized Task Scheduling in Distributed Systems: A Deep Reinforcement Learning Approach
Authors: Daniel Benniah John
First: 2026-03-25T18:59:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T18:59:45+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 8 figures. Under review. Code available at GitHub
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Efficient task scheduling in large-scale distributed systems presents significant challenges due to dynamic workloads, heterogeneous resources, and competing quality-of-service requirements. Traditional centralized approaches face scalability limitations and single points of failure, while classical heuristics lack adaptability to changing conditions. This paper proposes a decentralized multi-agent deep reinforcement learning (DRL-MADRL) framework for task scheduling in heterogeneous distributed systems. We formulate the problem as a Decentralized Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (Dec-POMDP) and develop a lightweight actor-critic architecture implemented using only NumPy, enabling deployment on resource-constrained edge devices without heavyweight machine learning frameworks. Using workload characteristics derived from the publicly available Google Cluster Trace dataset, we evaluate our approach on a 100-node heterogeneous system processing 1,000 tasks per episode over 30 experimental runs. Experimental results demonstrate 15.6% improvement in average task completion time (30.8s vs 36.5s for random baseline), 15.2% energy efficiency gain (745.2 kWh vs 878.3 kWh), and 82.3% SLA satisfaction compared to 75.5% for baselines, with all improvements statistically significant (p < 0.001). The lightweight implementation requires only NumPy, Matplotlib, and SciPy. Complete source code and experimental data are provided for full reproducibility at https://github.com/danielbenniah/marl-distributed-scheduling.
中文标题/摘要
标题：分布式系统中的去中心化任务调度：一种深度强化学习方法
大规模分布式系统中的高效任务调度因动态工作负载、异构资源及相互竞争的服务质量要求而面临重大挑战。传统集中式方法存在可扩展性限制和单点故障问题，而经典启发式算法缺乏对动态环境的适应性。本文提出一种用于异构分布式系统任务调度的去中心化多智能体深度强化学习框架。我们将该问题建模为去中心化部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程，并开发了仅使用NumPy实现的轻量级行动者-评论家架构，可在资源受限的边缘设备上部署而无需重量级机器学习框架。基于公开的Google集群追踪数据集提取工作负载特征，我们在100节点异构系统上进行了30次实验评估，每次实验处理1000个任务。实验结果显示：平均任务完成时间提升15.6%（30.8秒对比随机基线36.5秒），能效提升15.2%（745.2千瓦时对比878.3千瓦时），服务等级协议满足率达到82.3%（基线为75.5%），所有改进均具有统计显著性（p<0.001）。该轻量级实现仅需NumPy、Matplotlib和SciPy。完整源代码和实验数据已发布于https://github.com/danielbenniah/marl-distributed-scheduling，确保完全可复现性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of centralized schedulers and non-adaptive heuristics in dynamic, heterogeneous distributed systems, this paper proposes a decentralized multi-agent deep reinforcement learning framework (DRL-MADRL) for task scheduling, formulated as a Decentralized Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (Dec-POMDP). The method employs a lightweight actor-critic architecture implemented solely with NumPy to enable deployment on resource-constrained edge devices. Experimental evaluation on a 100-node system using Google Cluster Trace data shows statistically significant improvements, including a 15.6% reduction in average task completion time, a 15.2% gain in energy efficiency, and an 82.3% SLA satisfaction rate, outperforming baseline approaches.
针对动态异构分布式系统中集中式调度器可扩展性差和传统启发式方法适应性不足的问题，本文提出了一种基于去中心化多智能体深度强化学习（DRL-MADRL）的任务调度框架，将问题建模为去中心化部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（Dec-POMDP）。该方法采用轻量级的行动者-评论家架构，仅使用NumPy实现，以便部署在资源受限的边缘设备上。基于谷歌集群追踪数据在100节点系统上的实验结果表明，该方法在平均任务完成时间上提升了15.6%，能效提高了15.2%，服务等级协议满足率达到82.3%，所有改进均具有统计显著性，优于基线方法。
Training LLMs for Multi-Step Tool Orchestration with Constrained Data Synthesis and Graduated Rewards
Authors: Cheng Jiayang, Xin Liu, Zhihan Zhang, Haoyang Wen, Zixuan Zhang, Qingyu Yin, Shiyang Li, Priyanka Nigam, Bing Yin, Chao Zhang, Yangqiu Song
First: 2026-03-25T18:31:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T18:31:39+00:00
Comments: Under Review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-step tool orchestration, where LLMs must invoke multiple dependent APIs in the correct order while propagating intermediate outputs, remains challenging. State-of-the-art models frequently fail on full sequence execution, with parameter value errors accounting for a significant portion of failures. Training models to handle such workflows faces two obstacles: existing environments focus on simple per-turn function calls with simulated data, and binary rewards provide no signal for partial correctness. We present a framework addressing both challenges. First, we construct a reinforcement learning environment backed by a large-scale cache of real API responses, enabling a data synthesis pipeline that samples valid multi-step orchestration traces with controllable complexity and significantly higher generation efficiency than unconstrained methods. Second, we propose a graduated reward design that decomposes correctness into atomic validity (individual function call correctness at increasing granularity) and orchestration (correct tool sequencing with dependency respect). On ComplexFuncBench, our approach demonstrates substantial improvements in turn accuracy. Ablation studies confirm both reward components are essential: using either alone significantly degrades performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于受限数据合成与渐进式奖励的大语言模型多步骤工具编排训练
多步骤工具编排要求大语言模型按正确顺序调用多个依赖API并传递中间输出，目前仍具挑战性。前沿模型在执行完整序列时经常失败，其中参数值错误占失败案例的很大比例。训练模型处理此类工作流面临两大障碍：现有环境主要关注基于模拟数据的简单单轮函数调用，且二元奖励机制无法对部分正确性提供信号。 我们提出了一个同时解决这两个挑战的框架。首先，我们构建了一个由大规模真实API响应缓存支持的强化学习环境，实现了数据合成流程，可采样具有可控复杂度的有效多步骤编排轨迹，其生成效率显著高于无约束方法。其次，我们提出了一种渐进式奖励设计，将正确性分解为原子有效性（在递增粒度上评估单个函数调用的正确性）和编排正确性（遵循依赖关系的工具调用顺序）。在ComplexFuncBench基准测试中，我们的方法在轮次准确率上展现出显著提升。消融研究证实两个奖励组件均不可或缺：单独使用任一组件都会导致性能显著下降。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the challenge of training large language models (LLMs) for multi-step tool orchestration, where models must correctly sequence dependent API calls and propagate outputs, as current models often fail on full execution sequences. To address this, the method introduces a reinforcement learning environment with a large-scale cache of real API responses for efficient data synthesis of valid multi-step traces, alongside a graduated reward design that decomposes correctness into atomic validity and orchestration components. Experimental results on ComplexFuncBench show substantial improvements in turn accuracy, with ablation studies confirming that both reward components are essential for performance.
本文的动机在于训练大型语言模型进行多步骤工具编排的挑战，即模型需正确排序依赖的API调用并传递输出，而现有模型常在全序列执行中失败。为此，方法构建了一个基于大规模真实API响应缓存的强化学习环境，用于高效合成有效的多步骤轨迹，并提出了分级奖励设计，将正确性分解为原子有效性和编排正确性。在ComplexFuncBench上的实验结果表明，该方法在轮次准确性上取得了显著提升，消融研究证实两个奖励组件对性能均至关重要。
DreamerAD: Efficient Reinforcement Learning via Latent World Model for Autonomous Driving
Authors: Pengxuan Yang, Yupeng Zheng, Deheng Qian, Zebin Xing, Qichao Zhang, Linbo Wang, Yichen Zhang, Shaoyu Guo, Zhongpu Xia, Qiang Chen, Junyu Han, Lingyun Xu, Yifeng Pan, Dongbin Zhao
First: 2026-03-25T17:57:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T17:57:09+00:00
Comments: first version
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce DreamerAD, the first latent world model framework that enables efficient reinforcement learning for autonomous driving by compressing diffusion sampling from 100 steps to 1 - achieving 80x speedup while maintaining visual interpretability. Training RL policies on real-world driving data incurs prohibitive costs and safety risks. While existing pixel-level diffusion world models enable safe imagination-based training, they suffer from multi-step diffusion inference latency (2s/frame) that prevents high-frequency RL interaction. Our approach leverages denoised latent features from video generation models through three key mechanisms: (1) shortcut forcing that reduces sampling complexity via recursive multi-resolution step compression, (2) an autoregressive dense reward model operating directly on latent representations for fine-grained credit assignment, and (3) Gaussian vocabulary sampling for GRPO that constrains exploration to physically plausible trajectories. DreamerAD achieves 87.7 EPDMS on NavSim v2, establishing state-of-the-art performance and demonstrating that latent-space RL is effective for autonomous driving.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DreamerAD：基于潜在世界模型的高效自动驾驶强化学习框架
本文提出DreamerAD，首个通过将扩散采样从100步压缩至1步实现80倍加速的潜在世界模型框架，在保持视觉可解释性的同时实现高效自动驾驶强化学习。基于真实驾驶数据训练RL策略成本高昂且存在安全风险，现有像素级扩散世界模型虽支持基于想象的安全训练，但其多步扩散推理延迟（2秒/帧）阻碍了高频RL交互。本方法通过三项关键机制利用视频生成模型的去噪潜在特征：（1）通过递归多分辨率步长压缩降低采样复杂度的捷径强制机制；（2）直接在潜在表征上运行的自回归密集奖励模型，实现细粒度信用分配；（3）为GRPO设计的高斯词汇采样，将探索约束在物理可行的轨迹空间。DreamerAD在NavSim v2上取得87.7 EPDMS，确立最先进性能，证明潜在空间强化学习对自动驾驶的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces DreamerAD, a novel latent world model framework designed to address the high costs and safety risks of training reinforcement learning (RL) policies directly on real-world autonomous driving data. The method compresses diffusion sampling from 100 steps to just 1 step, achieving an 80x speedup, by leveraging denoised latent features through three key mechanisms: shortcut forcing for recursive multi-resolution step compression, an autoregressive dense reward model for fine-grained credit assignment in latent space, and Gaussian vocabulary sampling to constrain exploration to physically plausible trajectories. Experimental results demonstrate state-of-the-art performance, with DreamerAD achieving 87.7 EPDMS on the NavSim v2 benchmark, confirming the effectiveness of latent-space RL for autonomous driving while maintaining visual interpretability.
本文提出了DreamerAD，一种新颖的潜在世界模型框架，旨在解决直接在真实世界自动驾驶数据上训练强化学习策略所面临的高成本和安全风险。该方法通过利用去噪的潜在特征，将扩散采样从100步压缩至1步，实现了80倍的加速，其核心机制包括：通过递归多分辨率步长压缩的快捷强制、在潜在空间上运行用于细粒度信用分配的自回归密集奖励模型，以及约束探索于物理可行轨迹的高斯词汇采样。实验结果表明，DreamerAD在NavSim v2基准测试中取得了87.7 EPDMS的最先进性能，证实了潜在空间强化学习在自动驾驶中的有效性，同时保持了视觉可解释性。
VFIG: Vectorizing Complex Figures in SVG with Vision-Language Models
Authors: Qijia He, Xunmei Liu, Hammaad Memon, Ziang Li, Zixian Ma, Jaemin Cho, Jason Ren, Daniel S Weld, Ranjay Krishna
First: 2026-03-25T17:52:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T17:52:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Scalable Vector Graphics (SVG) are an essential format for technical illustration and digital design, offering precise resolution independence and flexible semantic editability. In practice, however, original vector source files are frequently lost or inaccessible, leaving only "flat" rasterized versions (e.g., PNG or JPEG) that are difficult to modify or scale. Manually reconstructing these figures is a prohibitively labor-intensive process, requiring specialized expertise to recover the original geometric intent. To bridge this gap, we propose VFIG, a family of Vision-Language Models trained for complex and high-fidelity figure-to-SVG conversion. While this task is inherently data-driven, existing datasets are typically small-scale and lack the complexity of professional diagrams. We address this by introducing VFIG-DATA, a large-scale dataset of 66K high-quality figure-SVG pairs, curated from a diverse mix of real-world paper figures and procedurally generated diagrams. Recognizing that SVGs are composed of recurring primitives and hierarchical local structures, we introduce a coarse-to-fine training curriculum that begins with supervised fine-tuning (SFT) to learn atomic primitives and transitions to reinforcement learning (RL) refinement to optimize global diagram fidelity, layout consistency, and topological edge cases. Finally, we introduce VFIG-BENCH, a comprehensive evaluation suite with novel metrics designed to measure the structural integrity of complex figures. VFIG achieves state-of-the-art performance among open-source models and performs on par with GPT-5.2, achieving a VLM-Judge score of 0.829 on VFIG-BENCH.
中文标题/摘要
标题：VFIG：基于视觉语言模型的复杂SVG图形矢量化技术
可缩放矢量图形（SVG）作为技术插图和数字设计的核心格式，具有精确的分辨率独立性与灵活的语义可编辑性。然而实践中，原始矢量源文件常丢失或不可获取，仅存难以修改或缩放的“扁平化”栅格版本（如PNG或JPEG）。手动重建这类图形需耗费大量人力且依赖专业经验以还原原始几何意图。为填补此空白，我们提出VFIG系列视觉语言模型，专门针对复杂高保真图形至SVG的转换任务进行训练。尽管该任务本质依赖数据驱动，现有数据集通常规模有限且缺乏专业图表的复杂性。为此我们构建了VFIG-DATA大规模数据集，包含6.6万组从真实论文图表与程序生成图表中精选的高质量图形-SVG配对数据。基于SVG由重复图元与分层局部结构构成的特点，我们设计了由粗到精的训练方案：先通过监督微调学习原子图元，再通过强化学习优化全局图表保真度、布局一致性与拓扑边缘案例。最后，我们推出VFIG-BENCH综合评估框架，其创新性指标专门用于衡量复杂图形的结构完整性。VFIG在开源模型中达到最先进性能，与GPT-5.2表现相当，在VFIG-BENCH上获得0.829的VLM-Judge评分。

The paper addresses the challenge of reconstructing scalable vector graphics (SVG) from rasterized figures, a task that is typically labor-intensive and requires specialized expertise when original vector files are lost. The authors propose VFIG, a family of vision-language models trained for high-fidelity figure-to-SVG conversion, supported by a new large-scale dataset, VFIG-DATA, containing 66K figure-SVG pairs from real-world and procedurally generated sources. Their method employs a coarse-to-fine training curriculum, starting with supervised fine-tuning to learn atomic primitives and transitioning to reinforcement learning to optimize global fidelity and layout. Experimental results show that VFIG achieves state-of-the-art performance among open-source models and matches GPT-5.2, with a VLM-Judge score of 0.829 on their comprehensive evaluation suite, VFIG-BENCH.
本文针对从栅格化图像重建可缩放矢量图形（SVG）的挑战，该任务在原始矢量文件丢失时通常需要大量人工和专业技巧。作者提出了VFIG，一个用于高保真图形到SVG转换的视觉语言模型系列，并引入了一个新的大规模数据集VFIG-DATA，包含来自真实世界和程序生成来源的66K个图形-SVG对。方法采用从粗到精的训练策略，从监督微调学习基本图元开始，过渡到强化学习以优化整体保真度和布局。实验结果表明，VFIG在开源模型中实现了最先进的性能，并与GPT-5.2相当，在其综合评估套件VFIG-BENCH上获得了0.829的VLM-Judge分数。
Completeness of Unbounded Best-First Minimax and Descent Minimax
Authors: Quentin Cohen-Solal
First: 2026-03-25T17:50:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T17:50:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this article, we focus on search algorithms for two-player perfect information games, whose objective is to determine the best possible strategy, and ideally a winning strategy. Unfortunately, some search algorithms for games in the literature are not able to always determine a winning strategy, even with an infinite search time. This is the case, for example, of the following algorithms: Unbounded Best-First Minimax and Descent Minimax, which are core algorithms in state-of-the-art knowledge-free reinforcement learning. They were then improved with the so-called completion technique. However, whether this technique sufficiently improves these algorithms to allow them to always determine a winning strategy remained an open question until now. To answer this question, we generalize the two algorithms (their versions using the completion technique), and we show that any algorithm of this class of algorithms computes the best strategy. Finally, we experimentally show that the completion technique improves winning performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无界最佳优先极小极大与下降极小极大的完备性
本文聚焦于双人完全信息博弈的搜索算法，其目标是确定最优策略（理想情况下为必胜策略）。然而，现有文献中的部分博弈搜索算法即使在无限搜索时间内也无法始终确定必胜策略，例如无界最佳优先极小极大算法与下降极小极大算法——这两者是当前无先验知识强化学习的核心算法。这些算法后续通过所谓“完备化技术”得到改进，但该技术是否足以使算法始终确定必胜策略，此前一直悬而未决。为解答此问题，我们推广了采用完备化技术的两种算法，证明该类算法中的任意算法均可计算出最优策略。最后，实验结果表明完备化技术显著提升了获胜性能。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the incompleteness of certain search algorithms in two-player perfect information games, specifically Unbounded Best-First Minimax and Descent Minimax, which cannot guarantee a winning strategy even with infinite time, despite their use in knowledge-free reinforcement learning. The method involves generalizing these algorithms with a completion technique and analyzing whether this enhancement ensures they can always compute the best strategy. The main experimental results demonstrate that the completion technique indeed improves winning performance, resolving the open question by showing that the generalized class of algorithms can determine optimal strategies.
本文的研究动机是解决双人完全信息游戏中某些搜索算法的不完备性问题，特别是无界最佳优先极小极大和下降极小极大算法，这些算法即使在无限时间内也无法保证找到必胜策略，尽管它们被用于无知识强化学习。研究方法包括通过完成技术对这些算法进行泛化，并分析这种改进是否能确保它们始终计算出最佳策略。主要实验结果表明，完成技术确实提高了获胜性能，通过证明泛化后的算法类能够确定最优策略，从而解决了这一开放性问题。
Trust Region Constrained Bayesian Optimization with Penalized Constraint Handling
Authors: Raju Chowdhury, Tanmay Sen, Prajamitra Bhuyan, Biswabrata Pradhan
First: 2026-03-25T17:44:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T17:44:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Constrained optimization in high-dimensional black-box settings is difficult due to expensive evaluations, the lack of gradient information, and complex feasibility regions. In this work, we propose a Bayesian optimization method that combines a penalty formulation, a surrogate model, and a trust region strategy. The constrained problem is converted to an unconstrained form by penalizing constraint violations, which provides a unified modeling framework. A trust region restricts the search to a local region around the current best solution, which improves stability and efficiency in high dimensions. Within this region, we use the Expected Improvement acquisition function to select evaluation points by balancing improvement and uncertainty. The proposed Trust Region method integrates penalty-based constraint handling with local surrogate modeling. This combination enables efficient exploration of feasible regions while maintaining sample efficiency. We compare the proposed method with state-of-the-art methods on synthetic and real-world high-dimensional constrained optimization problems. The results show that the method identifies high-quality feasible solutions with fewer evaluations and maintains stable performance across different settings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于惩罚约束处理的信赖域约束贝叶斯优化
高维黑盒约束优化因评估成本高、梯度信息缺失及可行域复杂而极具挑战。本研究提出一种贝叶斯优化方法，融合惩罚函数、代理模型与信赖域策略：通过惩罚约束违反将约束问题转化为无约束形式，构建统一建模框架；信赖域将搜索限制在当前最优解邻域，提升高维场景的稳定性与效率；在该区域内采用期望改进采集函数，通过平衡改进量与不确定性选择评估点。所提出的信赖域方法将基于惩罚的约束处理与局部代理建模相结合，在保持采样效率的同时实现对可行域的高效探索。通过在合成与真实高维约束优化问题上与前沿方法对比，结果表明该方法能以更少评估次数获得高质量可行解，并在不同场景下保持稳定性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of high-dimensional constrained black-box optimization, where evaluations are costly and gradients are unavailable, by proposing a Bayesian optimization method that integrates penalty-based constraint handling with a trust region strategy. The method converts the constrained problem into an unconstrained form by penalizing violations, uses a trust region to localize the search around the current best solution for stability, and applies the Expected Improvement acquisition function within this region to balance exploration and exploitation. Experimental results on synthetic and real-world problems demonstrate that the method achieves high-quality feasible solutions with fewer evaluations and maintains robust performance across various settings.
本文针对高维约束黑盒优化中评估成本高、梯度信息缺失的难题，提出了一种结合惩罚约束处理与信赖域策略的贝叶斯优化方法。该方法通过惩罚约束违反将问题转化为无约束形式，利用信赖域将搜索限制在当前最优解附近以提升稳定性，并在该区域内使用期望改进采集函数来平衡探索与利用。在合成和真实世界的高维约束优化问题上的实验结果表明，该方法能以更少的评估次数找到高质量的可行解，并在不同设置下保持稳定的性能。
The Free-Market Algorithm: Self-Organizing Optimization for Open-Ended Complex Systems
Authors: Martin Jaraiz
First: 2026-03-25T17:41:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T17:41:25+00:00
Comments: 26 pages, 3 figures, 2 tables, draft
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce the Free-Market Algorithm (FMA), a novel metaheuristic inspired by free-market economics. Unlike Genetic Algorithms, Particle Swarm Optimization, and Simulated Annealing -- which require prescribed fitness functions and fixed search spaces -- FMA uses distributed supply-and-demand dynamics where fitness is emergent, the search space is open-ended, and solutions take the form of hierarchical pathway networks. Autonomous agents discover rules, trade goods, open and close firms, and compete for demand with no centralized controller. FMA operates through a three-layer architecture: a universal market mechanism (supply, demand, competition, selection), pluggable domain-specific behavioral rules, and domain-specific observation. The market mechanism is identical across applications; only the behavioral rules change. Validated in two unrelated domains. In prebiotic chemistry, starting from 900 bare atoms (C, H, O, N), FMA discovers all 12 feasible amino acid formulas, all 5 nucleobases, the formose sugar chain, and Krebs cycle intermediates in under 5 minutes on a laptop -- with up to 240 independent synthesis routes per product. In macroeconomic forecasting, reading a single input-output table with zero estimated parameters, FMA achieves Mean Absolute Error of 0.42 percentage points for non-crisis GDP prediction, comparable to professional forecasters, portable to 33 countries. Assembly Theory alignment shows that FMA provides the first explicit, tunable mechanism for the selection signatures described by Sharma et al. (Nature, 2023). The event-driven assembly dynamics resonate with foundational programs in physics -- causal set theory, relational quantum mechanics, constructor theory -- suggesting that Darwinian market dynamics may reflect a deeper organizational principle that lead to the unfolding of Nature itself.
中文标题/摘要
标题：自由市场算法：面向开放式复杂系统的自组织优化方法
本文提出自由市场算法（FMA），一种受自由市场经济启发的元启发式算法。与遗传算法、粒子群优化和模拟退火等需要预设适应度函数和固定搜索空间的传统方法不同，FMA采用分布式供需动态机制：适应度是涌现的，搜索空间是开放式的，解以分层路径网络形式呈现。自主智能体通过发现规则、交易商品、开设/关闭企业、竞争需求实现完全去中心化运作。 FMA采用三层架构：通用市场机制（供给、需求、竞争、选择）、可插拔的领域特定行为规则、领域特定观测模块。市场机制在所有应用中保持统一，仅行为规则随领域变化。 算法在两个无关领域得到验证：在生命起源化学模拟中，从900个基础原子（C、H、O、N）出发，FMA在笔记本电脑5分钟内发现了全部12种可行氨基酸分子式、5种核碱基、甲醛糖链及克雷布斯循环中间体，每种产物最多生成240条独立合成路径；在宏观经济预测中，仅读取单张投入产出表且无需参数估计，FMA对非危机时期GDP预测的平均绝对误差达0.42个百分点，与专业预测机构相当，并可推广至33个国家。 组装理论对齐表明，FMA为Sharma等人（《自然》，2023）描述的选择特征提供了首个可调节的显式机制。其事件驱动的组装动力学与物理学基础理论（因果集理论、关系量子力学、构造器理论）产生共鸣，暗示达尔文式市场动态可能反映了导致自然本身展开的深层组织原则。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of traditional metaheuristics that rely on predefined fitness functions and fixed search spaces, this paper introduces the Free-Market Algorithm (FMA), a novel self-organizing optimization method inspired by free-market economics. The method employs a decentralized, three-layer architecture where autonomous agents interact through supply-and-demand dynamics to discover rules and form hierarchical networks without central control, with the core market mechanism remaining constant across applications while behavioral rules are domain-specific. Experimental results demonstrate its effectiveness in two distinct domains: in prebiotic chemistry, it rapidly discovers key biochemical compounds like amino acids and nucleobases along with numerous synthesis pathways from basic atoms, and in macroeconomic forecasting, it achieves accurate GDP predictions comparable to professional forecasts across multiple countries using minimal input data.
本文的动机是克服传统元启发式算法依赖预设适应度函数和固定搜索空间的局限，提出了一种受自由市场经济启发的新型自组织优化方法——自由市场算法。该方法采用去中心化的三层架构，自主代理通过供需动态交互来发现规则并形成分层网络，无需中央控制，其核心市场机制在不同应用中保持一致，仅行为规则随领域变化。主要实验结果表明，该算法在两个不同领域表现卓越：在生命起源化学中，它能从基本原子快速发现氨基酸、核碱基等关键生化物质及大量合成路径；在宏观经济预测中，仅使用少量输入数据即可实现与专业预测相媲美的GDP预测精度，并适用于多国数据。
KINESIS: Motion Imitation for Human Musculoskeletal Locomotion
Authors: Merkourios Simos, Alberto Silvio Chiappa, Alexander Mathis
Venue: ICRA
First: 2025-03-18T18:37:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T15:38:25+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICRA. Here we include an appendix
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
How do humans move? Advances in reinforcement learning (RL) have produced impressive results in capturing human motion using physics-based humanoid control. However, torque-controlled humanoids fail to model key aspects of human motor control such as biomechanical joint constraints & non-linear and overactuated musculotendon control. We present KINESIS, a model-free motion imitation framework that tackles these challenges. KINESIS is trained on 1.8 hours of locomotion data and achieves strong motion imitation performance on unseen trajectories. Through a negative mining approach, KINESIS learns robust locomotion priors that we leverage to deploy the policy on several downstream tasks such as text-to-control, target point reaching, and football penalty kicks. Importantly, KINESIS learns to generate muscle activity patterns that correlate well with human EMG activity. We show that these results scale seamlessly across biomechanical model complexity, demonstrating control of up to 290 muscles. Overall, the physiological plausibility makes KINESIS a promising model for tackling challenging problems in human motor control. Code, videos and benchmarks are available at https://github.com/amathislab/Kinesis.
中文标题/摘要
标题：KINESIS：面向人体肌肉骨骼运动的动作模仿框架
人类如何运动？强化学习（RL）的进展在基于物理的人形控制捕捉人体运动方面取得了显著成果。然而，扭矩控制的人形模型未能模拟人类运动控制的关键特征，如生物力学关节约束、非线性及过驱动的肌肉肌腱控制。本文提出KINESIS——一种无模型动作模仿框架以应对这些挑战。该框架基于1.8小时运动数据训练，在未见轨迹上实现了优异的动作模仿性能。通过负样本挖掘策略，KINESIS学习了鲁棒的运动先验知识，并成功应用于文本控制、目标点抵达、足球点球等下游任务。值得注意的是，KINESIS能生成与人类肌电活动高度相关的肌肉激活模式。实验表明该框架可无缝适配不同复杂度的生物力学模型，最高实现对290块肌肉的控制。其生理合理性使KINESIS成为解决人类运动控制难题的前沿模型。代码、视频及基准测试详见https://github.com/amathislab/Kinesis。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for KINESIS is to overcome the limitations of torque-controlled humanoids in modeling human motor control, such as biomechanical joint constraints and complex musculotendon dynamics. The method introduces a model-free motion imitation framework trained on 1.8 hours of locomotion data, utilizing a negative mining approach to learn robust locomotion priors. Experimental results show strong imitation performance on unseen trajectories, successful deployment in downstream tasks like text-to-control and target reaching, and the generation of muscle activity patterns that correlate well with human EMG, scaling effectively to control up to 290 muscles.
KINESIS的动机是克服扭矩控制人形机器人在模拟人类运动控制方面的局限性，如生物力学关节约束和复杂的肌肉肌腱动力学。该方法提出了一个基于1.8小时运动数据的无模型运动模仿框架，通过负样本挖掘学习鲁棒的运动先验。实验结果表明，该框架在未见轨迹上实现了强大的模仿性能，成功应用于文本到控制、目标点到达等下游任务，并能生成与人类肌电图活动高度相关的肌肉活动模式，可扩展控制多达290块肌肉。
Interactionless Inverse Reinforcement Learning: A Data-Centric Framework for Durable Alignment
Authors: Elias Malomgré, Pieter Simoens
First: 2026-02-16T15:40:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T15:10:39+00:00
Comments: Accepted for the AAMAS 2026 Blue Sky Ideas track
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
AI alignment is growing in importance, yet many current approaches learn safety behavior by directly modifying policy parameters, entangling normative constraints with the underlying policy. This often yields opaque, difficult-to-edit alignment artifacts and reduces their reuse across models or deployments, a failure mode we term Alignment Waste. We propose Interactionless Inverse Reinforcement Learning, a framework for learning inspectable, editable, and reusable reward artifacts separately from policy optimization. We further introduce the Alignment Flywheel, a human-in-the-loop lifecycle for iteratively auditing, patching, and hardening these artifacts through automated evaluation and refinement. Together, these ideas recast alignment from a disposable training expense into a durable, verifiable engineering asset.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无交互逆强化学习：一种面向持久对齐的数据中心化框架
人工智能对齐的重要性日益凸显，但当前许多方法通过直接修改策略参数来学习安全行为，将规范性约束与底层策略相耦合。这常导致产生不透明、难以编辑的对齐产物，并降低其在模型或部署间的复用性，我们称此失效模式为“对齐浪费”。我们提出无交互逆强化学习框架，旨在独立于策略优化过程，学习可检查、可编辑且可复用的奖励产物。进一步引入“对齐飞轮”——一种人机协同的生命周期，通过自动化评估与精化，迭代审计、修补和强化这些产物。这些理念共同将对齐从一次性的训练成本重塑为持久、可验证的工程资产。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the problem of Alignment Waste, where safety behaviors become entangled with policy parameters, making them opaque and non-reusable, this paper proposes a data-centric framework called Interactionless Inverse Reinforcement Learning. The method focuses on learning inspectable and editable reward artifacts separately from policy optimization, and introduces an iterative human-in-the-loop lifecycle called the Alignment Flywheel for auditing and refining these artifacts. The main experimental outcome is a conceptual framework that recasts alignment from a transient training cost into a durable, verifiable engineering asset, promoting reuse across models.
本文的动机是解决“对齐浪费”问题，即安全行为与策略参数纠缠导致其不透明且难以复用。为此，论文提出了一种名为“无交互逆强化学习”的数据中心框架，其方法是将可检查、可编辑的奖励构件与策略优化分离开来学习，并引入一个名为“对齐飞轮”的人机交互生命周期，用于通过自动评估和精化来迭代审计与加固这些构件。主要成果是提出了一个概念性框架，将对齐从一次性的训练开销转变为可持久化、可验证的工程资产，从而提升了跨模型的可复用性。
OffSim: Offline Simulator for Model-based Offline Inverse Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Woo-Jin Ahn, Sang-Ryul Baek, Yong-Jun Lee, Hyun-Duck Choi, Myo-Taeg Lim
First: 2025-10-17T10:07:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T15:07:48+00:00
Comments: Due to an authorship dispute among the co-authors, we request to withdraw this submission. The issue is currently unresolved, and we believe withdrawal is appropriate until the matter is settled
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning algorithms typically utilize an interactive simulator (i.e., environment) with a predefined reward function for policy training. Developing such simulators and manually defining reward functions, however, is often time-consuming and labor-intensive. To address this, we propose an Offline Simulator (OffSim), a novel model-based offline inverse reinforcement learning (IRL) framework, to emulate environmental dynamics and reward structure directly from expert-generated state-action trajectories. OffSim jointly optimizes a high-entropy transition model and an IRL-based reward function to enhance exploration and improve the generalizability of the learned reward. Leveraging these learned components, OffSim can subsequently train a policy offline without further interaction with the real environment. Additionally, we introduce OffSim$^+$, an extension that incorporates a marginal reward for multi-dataset settings to enhance exploration. Extensive MuJoCo experiments demonstrate that OffSim achieves substantial performance gains over existing offline IRL methods, confirming its efficacy and robustness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：OffSim：基于模型的离线逆强化学习离线模拟器
强化学习算法通常依赖带有预定义奖励函数的交互式模拟器（即环境）进行策略训练。然而，开发此类模拟器并手动定义奖励函数往往耗时费力。为此，我们提出离线模拟器（OffSim），一种新颖的基于模型的离线逆强化学习框架，可直接从专家生成的状态-动作轨迹中模拟环境动态和奖励结构。OffSim联合优化高熵转移模型和基于逆强化学习的奖励函数，以增强探索性并提升所学奖励的泛化能力。利用这些学习到的组件，OffSim随后可在无需与真实环境进一步交互的情况下离线训练策略。此外，我们引入OffSim⁺扩展版本，该版本在多数据集设置中引入边际奖励以加强探索。大量MuJoCo实验表明，OffSim相比现有离线逆强化学习方法取得显著性能提升，证实了其有效性和鲁棒性。

The motivation for this work is to overcome the time-consuming and labor-intensive process of developing interactive simulators and manually defining reward functions for reinforcement learning. The proposed method, OffSim, is a model-based offline inverse reinforcement learning framework that jointly learns a high-entropy transition model and a reward function directly from expert trajectories, with an extension called OffSim+ that adds a marginal reward for multi-dataset settings to enhance exploration. Experimental results on MuJoCo benchmarks show that OffSim achieves substantial performance gains over existing offline IRL methods, demonstrating its efficacy and robustness in training policies offline without further environment interaction.

CoordLight: Learning Decentralized Coordination for Network-Wide Traffic Signal Control
Authors: Yifeng Zhang, Harsh Goel, Peizhuo Li, Mehul Damani, Sandeep Chinchali, Guillaume Sartoretti
First: 2026-03-25T14:46:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T14:46:31+00:00
Comments: \c{opyright} 20XX IEEE. Personal use of this material is permitted. Permission from IEEE must be obtained for all other uses, in any current or future media, including reprinting/republishing this material for advertising or promotional purposes, creating new collective works, for resale or redistribution to servers or lists, or reuse of any copyrighted component of this work in other works
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Adaptive traffic signal control (ATSC) is crucial in alleviating congestion, maximizing throughput and promoting sustainable mobility in ever-expanding cities. Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) has recently shown significant potential in addressing complex traffic dynamics, but the intricacies of partial observability and coordination in decentralized environments still remain key challenges in formulating scalable and efficient control strategies. To address these challenges, we present CoordLight, a MARL-based framework designed to improve intra-neighborhood traffic by enhancing decision-making at individual junctions (agents), as well as coordination with neighboring agents, thereby scaling up to network-level traffic optimization. Specifically, we introduce the Queue Dynamic State Encoding (QDSE), a novel state representation based on vehicle queuing models, which strengthens the agents' capability to analyze, predict, and respond to local traffic dynamics. We further propose an advanced MARL algorithm, named Neighbor-aware Policy Optimization (NAPO). It integrates an attention mechanism that discerns the state and action dependencies among adjacent agents, aiming to facilitate more coordinated decision-making, and to improve policy learning updates through robust advantage calculation. This enables agents to identify and prioritize crucial interactions with influential neighbors, thus enhancing the targeted coordination and collaboration among agents. Through comprehensive evaluations against state-of-the-art traffic signal control methods over three real-world traffic datasets composed of up to 196 intersections, we empirically show that CoordLight consistently exhibits superior performance across diverse traffic networks with varying traffic flows. The code is available at https://github.com/marmotlab/CoordLight
中文标题/摘要
标题：CoordLight：学习去中心化协调以实现全网交通信号控制
自适应交通信号控制（ATSC）对于缓解不断扩张城市中的交通拥堵、最大化通行能力及促进可持续出行至关重要。多智能体强化学习（MARL）近期在处理复杂交通动态方面展现出巨大潜力，但去中心化环境中的部分可观测性与协调复杂性仍是构建可扩展高效控制策略的核心挑战。为此，我们提出CoordLight——一个基于MARL的框架，通过增强单个交叉口（智能体）的决策能力以及与相邻智能体的协调机制，实现从局部到全网级的交通优化。具体而言，我们引入基于车辆排队模型的队列动态状态编码（QDSE）这一新型状态表征方法，强化智能体分析、预测和响应局部交通动态的能力。进一步提出名为邻域感知策略优化（NAPO）的先进MARL算法，该算法集成注意力机制以识别相邻智能体间的状态与动作依赖关系，旨在促进更协调的决策，并通过鲁棒优势计算改进策略学习更新。这使得智能体能识别并优先处理与关键相邻节点的交互，从而增强智能体间的定向协调协作。通过在包含多达196个交叉口的三个真实交通数据集上，与前沿交通信号控制方法进行综合评估，我们实证表明CoordLight在不同交通流量的多样化路网中均表现出优越性能。代码发布于https://github.com/marmotlab/CoordLight

The paper addresses the challenges of partial observability and coordination in decentralized multi-agent reinforcement learning for adaptive traffic signal control, aiming to alleviate urban congestion and optimize network-wide traffic flow. The proposed CoordLight framework introduces a novel Queue Dynamic State Encoding for improved local traffic analysis and a Neighbor-aware Policy Optimization algorithm that uses an attention mechanism to model dependencies between adjacent intersections for coordinated decision-making. Experimental results on three real-world datasets with up to 196 intersections demonstrate that CoordLight consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods across diverse traffic conditions.
该论文针对去中心化多智能体强化学习在自适应交通信号控制中存在的部分可观测性和协调性挑战，旨在缓解城市拥堵并优化全网交通流。提出的CoordLight框架引入了新颖的队列动态状态编码以增强局部交通分析能力，并采用基于注意力机制的邻居感知策略优化算法来建模相邻路口间的依赖关系，从而实现协调决策。在包含多达196个交叉路口的三个真实世界交通数据集上的实验结果表明，CoordLight在不同交通条件下均持续优于现有先进方法。
AceGRPO: Adaptive Curriculum Enhanced Group Relative Policy Optimization for Autonomous Machine Learning Engineering
Authors: Yuzhu Cai, Zexi Liu, Xinyu Zhu, Cheng Wang, Siheng Chen
First: 2026-02-08T10:55:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T14:38:58+00:00
Comments: 17 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Autonomous Machine Learning Engineering (MLE) requires agents to perform sustained, iterative optimization over long horizons. While recent LLM-based agents show promise, current prompt-based agents for MLE suffer from behavioral stagnation due to frozen parameters. Although Reinforcement Learning (RL) offers a remedy, applying it to MLE is hindered by prohibitive execution latency and inefficient data selection. Recognizing these challenges, we propose AceGRPO with two core components: (1) Evolving Data Buffer that continuously repurposes execution traces into reusable training tasks, and (2) Adaptive Sampling guided by a Learnability Potential function, which dynamically prioritizes tasks at the agent's learning frontier to maximize learning efficiency. Leveraging AceGRPO, our trained Ace-30B model achieves a 100% valid submission rate on MLE-Bench-Lite, approaches the performance of proprietary frontier models, and outperforms larger open-source baselines (e.g., DeepSeek-V3.2), demonstrating robust capability for sustained iterative optimization. Code is available at https://github.com/yuzhu-cai/AceGRPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AceGRPO：面向自主机器学习工程的自适应课程增强型群体相对策略优化
自主机器学习工程（MLE）要求智能体在长周期内执行持续迭代优化。尽管当前基于大语言模型的智能体展现出潜力，但现有基于提示的MLE智能体因参数冻结而存在行为停滞问题。强化学习虽能提供解决方案，但其在MLE中的应用受限于高昂的执行延迟和低效的数据选择。针对这些挑战，我们提出AceGRPO框架，其包含两大核心组件：（1）演化数据缓冲池——持续将执行轨迹转化为可复用的训练任务；（2）基于可学习性潜力函数的自适应采样机制——动态聚焦于智能体学习前沿的任务以最大化学习效率。基于AceGRPO训练的Ace-30B模型在MLE-Bench-Lite基准上实现100%有效提交率，性能接近前沿闭源模型，并超越更大规模的开源基线模型（如DeepSeek-V3.2），展现出持续迭代优化的强大能力。代码已开源：https://github.com/yuzhu-cai/AceGRPO。

The paper addresses the challenge of behavioral stagnation in prompt-based agents for Autonomous Machine Learning Engineering (MLE), where frozen parameters limit sustained iterative optimization. To overcome this, the authors propose AceGRPO, a method featuring an Evolving Data Buffer that repurposes execution traces into reusable tasks and an Adaptive Sampling mechanism guided by a Learnability Potential function to prioritize tasks at the learning frontier for efficiency. 本文针对自主机器学习工程中基于提示的智能体因参数冻结导致行为停滞、难以持续迭代优化的问题，提出AceGRPO方法。该方法包含两个核心组件：一是演化数据缓冲区，将执行轨迹转化为可重用的训练任务；二是基于可学习性潜力函数的自适应采样机制，动态优先选择智能体学习前沿的任务以最大化学习效率。实验结果表明，训练后的Ace-30B模型在MLE-Bench-Lite上实现了100%的有效提交率，性能接近专有前沿模型，并超越了如DeepSeek-V3.2等更大的开源基线，展现出强大的持续迭代优化能力。
Unicorn: A Universal and Collaborative Reinforcement Learning Approach Towards Generalizable Network-Wide Traffic Signal Control
Authors: Yifeng Zhang, Yilin Liu, Ping Gong, Peizhuo Li, Mingfeng Fan, Guillaume Sartoretti
First: 2025-03-14T15:13:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T14:38:45+00:00
Comments: \c{opyright} 20XX IEEE. Personal use of this material is permitted. Permission from IEEE must be obtained for all other uses, in any current or future media, including reprinting/republishing this material for advertising or promotional purposes, creating new collective works, for resale or redistribution to servers or lists, or reuse of any copyrighted component of this work in other works
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Adaptive traffic signal control (ATSC) is crucial in reducing congestion, maximizing throughput, and improving mobility in rapidly growing urban areas. Recent advancements in parameter-sharing multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) have greatly enhanced the scalable and adaptive optimization of complex, dynamic flows in large-scale homogeneous networks. However, the inherent heterogeneity of real-world traffic networks, with their varied intersection topologies and interaction dynamics, poses substantial challenges to achieving scalable and effective ATSC across different traffic scenarios. To address these challenges, we present Unicorn, a universal and collaborative MARL framework designed for efficient and adaptable network-wide ATSC. Specifically, we first propose a unified approach to map the states and actions of intersections with varying topologies into a common structure based on traffic movements. Next, we design a Universal Traffic Representation (UTR) module with a decoder-only network for general feature extraction, enhancing the model's adaptability to diverse traffic scenarios. Additionally, we incorporate an Intersection Specifics Representation (ISR) module, designed to identify key latent vectors that represent the unique intersection's topology and traffic dynamics through variational inference techniques. To further refine these latent representations, we employ a contrastive learning approach in a self-supervised manner, which enables better differentiation of intersection-specific features. Moreover, we integrate the state-action dependencies of neighboring agents into policy optimization, which effectively captures dynamic agent interactions and facilitates efficient regional collaboration. [...]. The code is available at https://github.com/marmotlab/Unicorn
中文标题/摘要
标题：Unicorn：一种面向通用化全网交通信号控制的通用协作强化学习方法
自适应交通信号控制（ATSC）对于缓解快速发展的城市区域拥堵、最大化通行能力和提升交通流动性至关重要。近年来，参数共享多智能体强化学习（MARL）的进展显著提升了大规模同质网络中复杂动态流量的可扩展自适应优化能力。然而，现实交通网络固有的异质性——包括多样化的交叉口拓扑结构和交互动态——给在不同交通场景中实现可扩展且有效的ATSC带来了巨大挑战。为应对这些挑战，我们提出了Unicorn，这是一个专为高效、适应性强的全网ATSC设计的通用协作MARL框架。具体而言，我们首先提出一种统一方法，将不同拓扑结构的交叉口状态与动作基于交通流向映射到通用结构中。其次，我们设计了一个仅含解码器网络的通用交通表征（UTR）模块，用于通用特征提取，增强模型对多样化交通场景的适应能力。此外，我们引入了交叉口特性表征（ISR）模块，该模块通过变分推断技术识别表征特定交叉口拓扑与交通动态的关键潜向量。为进一步优化这些潜表征，我们采用自监督对比学习方法，以更好区分交叉口特异性特征。同时，我们将相邻智能体的状态-动作依赖关系整合到策略优化中，有效捕捉动态智能体交互并促进高效区域协作。[...]。代码发布于https://github.com/marmotlab/Unicorn
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Unicorn, a universal and collaborative multi-agent reinforcement learning framework designed to address the challenge of applying adaptive traffic signal control across heterogeneous real-world traffic networks with diverse intersection topologies and dynamics. The method involves mapping different intersections into a common structure, employing a Universal Traffic Representation module for general feature extraction, an Intersection Specifics Representation module using variational inference to capture unique intersection characteristics, and refining these with contrastive learning, while also integrating neighbor state-action dependencies for regional collaboration. Experimental results demonstrate that Unicorn achieves effective and scalable network-wide traffic signal control, showing improved adaptability and performance across varied traffic scenarios compared to prior approaches.

Large Language Model Guided Incentive Aware Reward Design for Cooperative Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Dogan Urgun, Gokhan Gungor
First: 2026-03-25T14:05:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T14:05:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Designing effective auxiliary rewards for cooperative multi-agent systems remains a precarious task; misaligned incentives risk inducing suboptimal coordination, especially where sparse task feedback fails to provide sufficient grounding. This study introduces an automated reward design framework that leverages large language models to synthesize executable reward programs from environment instrumentation. The procedure constrains candidate programs within a formal validity envelope and evaluates their efficacy by training policies from scratch under a fixed computational budget; selection depends exclusively on the sparse task return. The framework is evaluated across four distinct Overcooked-AI layouts characterized by varied corridor congestion, handoff dependencies, and structural asymmetries. Iterative search generations consistently yield superior task returns and delivery counts, with the most pronounced gains occurring in environments dominated by interaction bottlenecks. Diagnostic analysis of the synthesized shaping components indicates increased interdependence in action selection and improved signal alignment in coordination-intensive tasks. These results demonstrate that the search for objectivegrounded reward programs can mitigate the burden of manual engineering while producing shaping signals compatible with cooperative learning under finite budgets.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于大语言模型引导的激励感知奖励设计用于合作式多智能体强化学习
为合作式多智能体系统设计有效的辅助奖励仍是一项艰巨任务：激励错位易导致次优协作，尤其在稀疏任务反馈无法提供充分依据的场景中。本研究提出一种自动化奖励设计框架，利用大语言模型从环境监测数据中合成可执行的奖励程序。该流程将候选程序约束在形式化有效范围内，并通过固定计算预算下从头训练策略来评估其效能；选择完全依据稀疏的任务回报。该框架在四种具有不同走廊拥堵度、交接依赖性和结构不对称性的《 overcooked-AI》布局中进行评估。迭代搜索过程持续产生更优的任务回报与配送数量，在交互瓶颈主导的环境中增益最为显著。对合成奖励组件的诊断分析表明，动作选择的相互依赖性增强，且在协作密集型任务中信号对齐性得到改善。这些结果证明，基于客观依据的奖励程序搜索能减轻人工设计的负担，同时生成与有限预算下合作学习兼容的塑形信号。

TikZilla: Scaling Text-to-TikZ with High-Quality Data and Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Christian Greisinger, Steffen Eger
First: 2026-03-03T15:17:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T13:51:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to assist scientists across diverse workflows. A key challenge is generating high-quality figures from textual descriptions, often represented as TikZ programs that can be rendered as scientific images. Prior research has proposed a variety of datasets and modeling approaches for this task. However, existing datasets for Text-to-TikZ are too small and noisy to capture the complexity of TikZ, causing mismatches between text and rendered figures. Moreover, prior approaches rely solely on supervised fine-tuning (SFT), which does not expose the model to the rendered semantics of the figure, often resulting in errors such as looping, irrelevant content, and incorrect spatial relations. To address these issues, we construct DaTikZ-V4, a dataset more than four times larger and substantially higher in quality than DaTikZ-V3, enriched with LLM-generated figure descriptions. Using this dataset, we train TikZilla, a family of small open-source Qwen models (3B and 8B) with a two-stage pipeline of SFT followed by reinforcement learning (RL). For RL, we leverage an image encoder trained via inverse graphics to provide semantically faithful reward signals. Extensive human evaluations with over 1,000 judgments show that TikZilla improves by 1.5-2 points over its base models on a 5-point scale, surpasses GPT-4o by 0.5 points, and matches GPT-5 in the image-based evaluation, while operating at much smaller model sizes. Code, data, and models will be made available.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TikZilla：通过高质量数据与强化学习实现文本到TikZ的规模化生成
大语言模型（LLMs）正日益广泛地应用于辅助科学家的多样化工作流程。其中，从文本描述生成高质量图表是一个关键挑战，这类描述通常以可渲染为科学图像的TikZ程序表示。先前研究已为此任务提出了多种数据集和建模方法。然而，现有的文本到TikZ数据集规模过小且噪声较多，难以捕捉TikZ的复杂性，导致文本与渲染图像之间存在不匹配。此外，现有方法仅依赖监督微调（SFT），未让模型接触图像的渲染语义，常产生循环结构、无关内容或空间关系错误等问题。为解决这些问题，我们构建了DaTikZ-V4数据集，其规模是DaTikZ-V3的四倍以上，质量显著提升，并融合了LLM生成的图像描述。基于此数据集，我们训练了TikZilla系列模型——采用3B和8B参数的小型开源Qwen模型，通过SFT后接强化学习（RL）的两阶段流程进行训练。在RL阶段，我们利用通过逆向图形训练的图像编码器提供语义保真的奖励信号。基于超1,000条判断的广泛人工评估表明，TikZilla在5分制评分中较基础模型提升1.5-2分，超越GPT-4o 0.5分，在基于图像的评估中与GPT-5表现相当，且模型规模显著更小。代码、数据及模型将公开提供。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of generating accurate scientific figures from text descriptions using TikZ code, noting that existing datasets are too small and noisy, and supervised fine-tuning alone fails to capture rendered figure semantics, leading to errors like looping and spatial inaccuracies. Experimental results from human evaluations with over 1,000 judgments show that TikZilla improves by 1.5-2 points over base models on a 5-point scale, surpasses GPT-4o by 0.5 points, and matches GPT-5 in image-based evaluation, despite operating at much smaller model sizes.
