标题：一种用于双层强化学习的无Hessian行动者-评论家算法及其在大语言模型微调中的应用
本文研究一个结构化双层优化问题，其中上层目标为光滑函数，下层问题为马尔可夫决策过程中的策略优化。上层决策变量参数化下层MDP的奖励函数，上层目标取决于诱导的最优策略。现有双层优化与强化学习方法常需二阶信息、对下层施加强正则化，或通过嵌套循环流程低效使用样本。本研究提出一种单循环一阶行动者-评论家算法，通过基于惩罚的重构优化双层目标。我们在下层RL目标中引入衰减熵正则化，使得无需精确求解无正则化RL问题即可实现渐近无偏的上层超梯度估计。通过特殊类型的Polyak-Lojasiewicz条件下新颖的下层残差分析，我们证明了所提算法在有限时间和有限样本内收敛至原始无正则化双层优化问题的稳定点。通过GridWorld目标定位任务和基于人类反馈强化学习的积极推文生成实验，验证了方法的有效性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the computational challenges of bi-level reinforcement learning, where an upper-level objective depends on the optimal policy of a lower-level Markov decision process whose reward is parameterized by the upper variable. The motivation is to overcome the need for second-order information, strong regularization, or inefficient nested loops in existing methods. The proposed method is a single-loop, first-order actor-critic algorithm that uses a penalty-based reformulation with an attenuating entropy regularization in the lower-level RL, enabling asymptotically unbiased hyper-gradient estimation without exact policy convergence. Experimental results on a GridWorld task and RLHF for happy tweet generation demonstrate the algorithm's effectiveness, with theoretical convergence guarantees to a stationary point under a Polyak-Lojasiewicz condition.
本文针对双层强化学习中的计算挑战展开研究，其中上层目标依赖于下层马尔可夫决策过程的最优策略，且下层奖励由上层的参数化变量决定。研究动机是克服现有方法对二阶信息、强正则化或低效嵌套循环的需求。所提出的方法是一种单循环、一阶的演员-评论家算法，采用基于惩罚的重构方法，并在下层强化学习中引入衰减的熵正则化，从而无需精确求解策略即可实现渐近无偏的超梯度估计。在GridWorld目标定位任务和基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）生成快乐推文的实验中验证了算法的有效性，并在Polyak-Lojasiewicz条件下提供了收敛到原问题稳定点的理论保证。
Off-Policy Safe Reinforcement Learning with Constrained Optimistic Exploration
Authors: Guopeng Li, Matthijs T. J. Spaan, Julian F. P. Kooij
Venue: ICLR 2026 poster
First: 2026-03-25T03:27:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T03:27:37+00:00
Comments: 21 pages, 9 figures, accepted by ICLR 2026 poster
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
When safety is formulated as a limit of cumulative cost, safe reinforcement learning (RL) aims to learn policies that maximize return subject to the cost constraint in data collection and deployment. Off-policy safe RL methods, although offering high sample efficiency, suffer from constraint violations due to cost-agnostic exploration and estimation bias in cumulative cost. To address this issue, we propose Constrained Optimistic eXploration Q-learning (COX-Q), an off-policy safe RL algorithm that integrates cost-bounded online exploration and conservative offline distributional value learning. First, we introduce a novel cost-constrained optimistic exploration strategy that resolves gradient conflicts between reward and cost in the action space and adaptively adjusts the trust region to control the training cost. Second, we adopt truncated quantile critics to stabilize the cost value learning. Quantile critics also quantify epistemic uncertainty to guide exploration. Experiments on safe velocity, safe navigation, and autonomous driving tasks demonstrate that COX-Q achieves high sample efficiency, competitive test safety performance, and controlled data collection cost. The results highlight COX-Q as a promising RL method for safety-critical applications.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于约束乐观探索的离策略安全强化学习
当安全性被表述为累积成本的上限时，安全强化学习（RL）的目标是在数据收集和部署过程中，学习在成本约束下最大化回报的策略。离策略安全RL方法虽然具有较高的样本效率，但由于成本无关的探索和累积成本的估计偏差，容易导致约束违反。为解决这一问题，我们提出了约束乐观探索Q学习（COX-Q），这是一种集成成本有界在线探索与保守离线分布价值学习的离策略安全RL算法。首先，我们引入了一种新颖的成本约束乐观探索策略，该策略解决了动作空间中奖励与成本的梯度冲突，并自适应调整信任区域以控制训练成本。其次，我们采用截断分位数评论器来稳定成本价值学习。分位数评论器还能量化认知不确定性以指导探索。在安全速度控制、安全导航和自动驾驶任务上的实验表明，COX-Q实现了高样本效率、具有竞争力的测试安全性能以及可控的数据收集成本。这些结果凸显了COX-Q作为安全关键应用领域一种有前景的RL方法。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of constraint violations in off-policy safe reinforcement learning (RL), which arise from cost-agnostic exploration and estimation bias in cumulative cost. To mitigate this, the authors propose Constrained Optimistic eXploration Q-learning (COX-Q), a method that combines cost-bounded online exploration with conservative offline distributional value learning using truncated quantile critics to stabilize cost value estimation and guide exploration via epistemic uncertainty. Experimental results on safe velocity, navigation, and autonomous driving tasks show that COX-Q achieves high sample efficiency, competitive safety performance during testing, and controlled data collection costs, positioning it as a promising approach for safety-critical applications.
本文针对离线策略安全强化学习中因成本无关探索和累积成本估计偏差导致的约束违反问题，提出了约束乐观探索Q学习（COX-Q）算法。该方法通过结合成本约束的在线探索与基于截断分位数评论家的保守离线分布价值学习，以稳定成本价值估计并利用认知不确定性指导探索。在安全速度控制、安全导航和自动驾驶任务上的实验表明，COX-Q实现了高样本效率、具有竞争力的测试安全性能以及受控的数据收集成本，突显了其在安全关键应用中的潜力。
The DeepXube Software Package for Solving Pathfinding Problems with Learned Heuristic Functions and Search
Authors: Forest Agostinelli
First: 2026-03-25T03:02:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T03:02:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
DeepXube is a free and open-source Python package and command-line tool that seeks to automate the solution of pathfinding problems by using machine learning to learn heuristic functions that guide heuristic search algorithms tailored to deep neural networks (DNNs). DeepXube is comprised of the latest advances in deep reinforcement learning, heuristic search, and formal logic for solving pathfinding problems. This includes limited-horizon Bellman-based learning, hindsight experience replay, batched heuristic search, and specifying goals with answer-set programming. A robust multiple-inheritance structure simplifies the definition of pathfinding domains and the generation of training data. Training heuristic functions is made efficient through the automatic parallelization of the generation of training data across central processing units (CPUs) and reinforcement learning updates across graphics processing units (GPUs). Pathfinding algorithms that take advantage of the parallelism of GPUs and DNN architectures, such as batch weighted A* and Q* search and beam search are easily employed to solve pathfinding problems through command-line arguments. Finally, several convenient features for visualization, code profiling, and progress monitoring during training and solving are available. The GitHub repository is publicly available at https://github.com/forestagostinelli/deepxube.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DeepXube软件包：利用学习启发式函数与搜索解决路径规划问题
DeepXube是一款免费开源的Python软件包及命令行工具，旨在通过机器学习学习启发式函数，以指导专为深度神经网络（DNN）设计的启发式搜索算法，从而自动化解决路径规划问题。该工具集成了深度强化学习、启发式搜索和形式逻辑领域的最新进展，包括基于有限视野贝尔曼方程的学习、后见经验回放、批处理启发式搜索以及使用答案集编程定义目标。其稳健的多重继承结构简化了路径规划领域的定义与训练数据生成。通过跨中央处理器（CPU）自动并行生成训练数据，并结合跨图形处理器（GPU）的强化学习更新，实现了启发式函数的高效训练。利用GPU并行性与DNN架构的路径规划算法（如批量加权A*搜索、Q*搜索和束搜索）可通过命令行参数轻松调用以解决问题。此外，该工具还提供训练与求解过程中的可视化、代码性能分析和进度监控等便捷功能。GitHub仓库公开地址为：https://github.com/forestagostinelli/deepxube。
Summary / 总结
The DeepXube software package is motivated by the need to automate the solution of pathfinding problems through learned heuristic functions, integrating advances in deep reinforcement learning, heuristic search, and formal logic. Its method employs techniques such as limited-horizon Bellman-based learning, hindsight experience replay, and batched heuristic search, with a robust multiple-inheritance structure for domain definition and efficient parallelized training across CPUs and GPUs. Experimental results demonstrate that the package enables effective solving of pathfinding problems using GPU-accelerated algorithms like batch weighted A* and Q* search, supported by features for visualization and progress monitoring.
DeepXube软件包的开发动机是通过学习启发式函数来自动解决路径规划问题，它整合了深度强化学习、启发式搜索和形式逻辑的最新进展。其方法采用了有限范围贝尔曼学习、后见经验回放和批处理启发式搜索等技术，通过健壮的多重继承结构定义领域，并利用CPU和GPU实现高效的并行化训练。实验结果表明，该软件包能够使用GPU加速算法（如批量加权A*和Q*搜索）有效解决路径规划问题，同时提供可视化和进度监控等便利功能。
HDPO: Hybrid Distillation Policy Optimization via Privileged Self-Distillation
Authors: Ken Ding
First: 2026-03-25T02:59:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T02:59:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models trained with reinforcement learning (RL) for mathematical reasoning face a fundamental challenge: on problems the model cannot solve at all - "cliff" prompts - the RL gradient vanishes entirely, preventing any learning signal from reaching these failure modes. We introduce Hybrid Distillation Policy Optimization (HDPO), which augments standard RL with privileged self-distillation targeting cliff prompts. On each training step, HDPO identifies prompts where all rollouts fail, generates privileged rollouts by providing the model with ground-truth information, filters for correct solutions, and distills the teacher's token-level distribution into the student. Because teacher and student share the same weights - differing only in their input - the realizability gap is provably bounded, unlike cross-model distillation. We prove that R=1 filtered privileged generation recovers the optimal KL-regularized RL policy in the hard-threshold limit. Experiments on OpenMathInstruct-2 with Qwen2.5-Math-1.5B-Instruct show that HDPO consistently improves coverage metrics (pass@4 by +0.8-1.1%, pass@8 by +0.4-1.7%) while maintaining greedy accuracy, with the distillation weight lambda providing direct control over the exploration-exploitation tradeoff.
中文标题/摘要
标题：HDPO：基于特权自蒸馏的混合蒸馏策略优化
采用强化学习训练的大语言模型在数学推理任务中面临根本性挑战：对于模型完全无法解决的“悬崖”提示，强化学习梯度完全消失，导致这些失败模式无法获得任何学习信号。本文提出混合蒸馏策略优化方法，通过针对悬崖提示的特权自蒸馏增强标准强化学习。在每轮训练中，HDPO识别所有轨迹均失败的提示，通过向模型提供真实信息生成特权轨迹，筛选正确解，并将教师的词元级分布蒸馏至学生模型。由于师生模型共享权重（仅输入不同），与跨模型蒸馏不同，其实现差距可证明是有界的。我们证明在硬阈值极限下，R=1过滤特权生成可恢复最优KL正则化强化学习策略。在OpenMathInstruct-2数据集使用Qwen2.5-Math-1.5B-Instruct模型的实验表明，HDPO在保持贪婪准确率的同时持续提升覆盖指标（pass@4提升0.8-1.1%，pass@8提升0.4-1.7%），蒸馏权重λ为探索-利用权衡提供直接控制。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge in RL-trained LLMs for math reasoning where vanishing gradients on unsolvable 'cliff' prompts prevent learning. It introduces HDPO, a method that augments RL with privileged self-distillation: it identifies failed prompts, generates privileged rollouts using ground-truth information, filters for correct solutions, and distills the teacher's token distributions into the student model, which shares weights with the teacher to bound the realizability gap. Theoretically, it shows filtered privileged generation recovers the optimal KL-regularized policy. Experiments on OpenMathInstruct-2 with Qwen2.5-Math-1.5B-Instruct demonstrate consistent improvements in coverage metrics (e.g., pass@4 by +0.8-1.1%) while maintaining greedy accuracy, with a distillation weight controlling exploration-exploitation tradeoffs.
该论文针对强化学习训练的大型语言模型在数学推理中遇到的挑战：在完全无法解决的“悬崖”提示上，梯度消失导致学习信号缺失。方法上提出了混合蒸馏策略优化（HDPO），通过特权自蒸馏增强标准强化学习：识别失败提示，利用真实信息生成特权轨迹，筛选正确解，并将教师的令牌级分布蒸馏到学生模型中，由于师生共享权重，可实现性差距有界。理论证明过滤后的特权生成可恢复最优KL正则化策略。在OpenMathInstruct-2数据集和Qwen2.5-Math-1.5B-Instruct模型上的实验表明，HDPO持续提升了覆盖率指标（如pass@4提高0.8-1.1%），同时保持贪婪准确率，蒸馏权重直接控制探索与利用的权衡。
Learning-guided Prioritized Planning for Lifelong Multi-Agent Path Finding in Warehouse Automation
Authors: Han Zheng, Yining Ma, Brandon Araki, Jingkai Chen, Cathy Wu
Venue: Journal of Artificial Intelligence Research, Vol. 85, Article 28. Publication date: March 2026
First: 2026-03-25T01:46:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T01:46:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Lifelong Multi-Agent Path Finding (MAPF) is critical for modern warehouse automation, which requires multiple robots to continuously navigate conflict-free paths to optimize the overall system throughput. However, the complexity of warehouse environments and the long-term dynamics of lifelong MAPF often demand costly adaptations to classical search-based solvers. While machine learning methods have been explored, their superiority over search-based methods remains inconclusive. In this paper, we introduce Reinforcement Learning (RL) guided Rolling Horizon Prioritized Planning (RL-RH-PP), the first framework integrating RL with search-based planning for lifelong MAPF. Specifically, we leverage classical Prioritized Planning (PP) as a backbone for its simplicity and flexibility in integrating with a learning-based priority assignment policy. By formulating dynamic priority assignment as a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP), RL-RH-PP exploits the sequential decision-making nature of lifelong planning while delegating complex spatial-temporal interactions among agents to reinforcement learning. An attention-based neural network autoregressively decodes priority orders on-the-fly, enabling efficient sequential single-agent planning by the PP planner. Evaluations in realistic warehouse simulations show that RL-RH-PP achieves the highest total throughput among baselines and generalizes effectively across agent densities, planning horizons, and warehouse layouts. Our interpretive analyses reveal that RL-RH-PP proactively prioritizes congested agents and strategically redirects agents from congestion, easing traffic flow and boosting throughput. These findings highlight the potential of learning-guided approaches to augment traditional heuristics in modern warehouse automation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：仓库自动化中终身多智能体路径规划的强化学习引导优先级规划
终身多智能体路径规划（MAPF）对现代仓库自动化至关重要，它要求多个机器人持续规划无冲突路径以优化系统整体吞吐量。然而，仓库环境的复杂性及终身MAPF的长期动态性常迫使传统基于搜索的求解器进行高成本调整。尽管机器学习方法已被探索，但其相对于搜索方法的优势尚未明确。本文提出强化学习引导的滚动时域优先级规划（RL-RH-PP），这是首个将强化学习与基于搜索的规划相结合用于终身MAPF的框架。具体而言，我们以经典优先级规划（PP）为骨干，利用其简洁性和灵活性集成基于学习的优先级分配策略。通过将动态优先级分配建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP），RL-RH-PP利用终身规划的序列决策特性，同时将智能体间复杂的时空交互交由强化学习处理。基于注意力的神经网络自回归地实时解码优先级序列，使PP规划器能高效执行序列化单智能体规划。在真实仓库仿真中的评估表明，RL-RH-PP在基线方法中实现了最高总吞吐量，并能有效适应不同智能体密度、规划时域和仓库布局。可解释性分析显示，RL-RH-PP主动优先处理拥堵智能体并策略性引导其绕行，从而缓解交通流并提升吞吐量。这些发现凸显了学习引导方法在现代仓库自动化中增强传统启发式算法的潜力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for efficient and adaptive lifelong Multi-Agent Path Finding (MAPF) in warehouse automation, where classical search-based solvers struggle with long-term dynamics, this paper introduces RL-RH-PP, a framework integrating Reinforcement Learning (RL) with Prioritized Planning. The method formulates dynamic priority assignment as a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP), using an attention-based neural network to autoregressively decode priority orders on-the-fly, which guides a classical PP planner for sequential single-agent planning. Experimental results in realistic warehouse simulations demonstrate that RL-RH-PP achieves the highest total throughput among baselines, generalizes well across varying agent densities, planning horizons, and layouts, and interpretively shows it proactively prioritizes congested agents to ease traffic flow.
本文针对仓库自动化中终身多智能体路径规划（MAPF）的长期动态复杂性，旨在克服传统基于搜索的求解器适应性成本高的问题，提出了RL-RH-PP框架，将强化学习与优先级规划相结合。该方法将动态优先级分配建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP），利用基于注意力的神经网络自回归地实时解码优先级顺序，从而指导经典的优先级规划器进行顺序单智能体规划。在真实仓库模拟中的实验结果表明，RL-RH-PP在基线方法中实现了最高的总吞吐量，能有效泛化到不同的智能体密度、规划视野和仓库布局，解释性分析显示其能主动优先处理拥堵智能体并策略性引导其绕行，从而缓解交通流并提升吞吐量。
Reward Is Enough: LLMs Are In-Context Reinforcement Learners
Authors: Kefan Song, Amir Moeini, Peng Wang, Lei Gong, Rohan Chandra, Shangtong Zhang, Yanjun Qi
First: 2025-05-21T16:15:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-25T00:04:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) is a framework for solving sequential decision-making problems. In this work, we demonstrate that, surprisingly, RL emerges during the inference time of large language models (LLMs), a phenomenon we term in-context RL (ICRL). To reveal this capability, we introduce a simple multi-round prompting framework, we call ICRL prompting, for inference-time self-improvement. The goal of ICRL prompting is to guide LLMs to perform reinforcement learning during inference for self-improvement on a given task. After each response, the model receives numerical scalar feedback, denoted as a reward. In the next round, we prompt the LLM again together with a context that concatenates all prior responses and their associated rewards. We consistently observe that response quality improves as the context grows. In other words, the LLM can optimize scalar reward signals during inference, exhibiting behavior analogous to reinforcement learning. We evaluate ICRL prompting on Game of 24, creative writing, ScienceWorld, and Olympiad-level math competitions (AIME and HMMT), demonstrating significant improvements over baselines such as Self-Refine and Reflexion. Notably, even when the reward signals are generated by the same LLM, ICRL prompting still improves performance, highlighting a promising new paradigm for test-time scaling.
中文标题/摘要
标题：奖励即足够：大语言模型是上下文强化学习者
强化学习（RL）是解决序列决策问题的框架。本研究发现，在大语言模型（LLM）的推理阶段会自发涌现强化学习行为，我们称之为上下文强化学习（ICRL）。为揭示此能力，我们提出了一个简单的多轮提示框架——ICRL提示法，用于实现推理时的自我改进。该方法旨在引导LLM在推理过程中通过强化学习优化特定任务表现：模型每轮生成响应后获得数值标量反馈（即奖励），下一轮提示时将包含所有历史响应及其对应奖励的上下文信息。实验表明，随着上下文扩展，响应质量持续提升——LLM能在推理过程中优化标量奖励信号，表现出类强化学习行为。我们在24点游戏、创意写作、ScienceWorld及奥林匹克数学竞赛（AIME与HMMT）上评估ICRL提示法，其性能显著优于Self-Refine、Reflexion等基线方法。值得注意的是，即使奖励信号由同一LLM生成，该方法仍能提升性能，这为测试时扩展提供了新的研究范式。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the hypothesis that reinforcement learning (RL) can emerge during the inference of large language models (LLMs) without explicit training, termed in-context RL (ICRL). The method introduces ICRL prompting, a multi-round framework where an LLM receives numerical scalar feedback (reward) after each response and is then reprompted with a context of prior responses and rewards to iteratively self-improve. Experimental results across tasks like Game of 24, creative writing, ScienceWorld, and math competitions show that response quality consistently improves with more rounds, outperforming baselines such as Self-Refine and Reflexion, even when rewards are generated by the same LLM, indicating a novel paradigm for test-time scaling.
本文的动机是假设强化学习（RL）可以在大型语言模型（LLM）的推理过程中自发涌现，无需显式训练，这被称为上下文强化学习（ICRL）。方法上提出了ICRL提示框架，通过多轮交互，让LLM在每次生成响应后接收数值标量反馈（奖励），并在下一轮提示中结合所有历史响应和奖励进行迭代自我优化。实验结果表明，在Game of 24、创意写作、ScienceWorld和数学竞赛等任务中，响应质量随轮次增加而持续提升，显著优于Self-Refine和Reflexion等基线方法，即使奖励由同一LLM生成也有效，这为测试时扩展提供了一种新范式。
Reward Engineering for Spatial Epidemic Simulations: A Reinforcement Learning Platform for Individual Behavioral Learning
Authors: Radman Rakhshandehroo, Daniel Coombs
Venue: Transactions on Machine Learning Research (TMLR), 2026
First: 2025-11-22T10:02:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T23:32:08+00:00
Comments: 38 pages, 15 figures and 18 tables; Accepted to TMLR. OpenReview: https://openreview.net/forum?id=yPEASsx3hk
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
We present ContagionRL, a Gymnasium-compatible reinforcement learning platform specifically designed for systematic reward engineering in spatial epidemic simulations. Unlike traditional agent-based models that rely on fixed behavioral rules, our platform enables rigorous evaluation of how reward function design affects learned survival strategies across diverse epidemic scenarios. ContagionRL integrates a spatial SIRS+D epidemiological model with configurable environmental parameters, allowing researchers to stress-test reward functions under varying conditions including limited observability, different movement patterns, and heterogeneous population dynamics. We evaluate five distinct reward designs, ranging from sparse survival bonuses to a novel potential field approach, across multiple RL algorithms (PPO, SAC, A2C). Through systematic ablation studies, we identify that directional guidance and explicit adherence incentives are critical components for robust policy learning. Our comprehensive evaluation across varying infection rates, grid sizes, visibility constraints, and movement patterns reveals that reward function choice dramatically impacts agent behavior and survival outcomes. Agents trained with our potential field reward consistently achieve superior performance, learning maximal adherence to non-pharmaceutical interventions while developing sophisticated spatial avoidance strategies. The platform's modular design enables systematic exploration of reward-behavior relationships, addressing a knowledge gap in models of this type where reward engineering has received limited attention. ContagionRL is an effective platform for studying adaptive behavioral responses in epidemic contexts and highlight the importance of reward design, information structure, and environmental predictability in learning. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/redradman/ContagionRL
中文标题/摘要
标题：空间流行病模拟中的奖励工程：面向个体行为学习的强化学习平台
我们提出了ContagionRL，这是一个兼容Gymnasium的强化学习平台，专门为空间流行病模拟中的系统性奖励工程而设计。与依赖固定行为规则的传统基于智能体的模型不同，我们的平台能够严格评估奖励函数设计如何影响不同疫情场景下习得的生存策略。ContagionRL集成了空间SIRS+D流行病学模型与可配置的环境参数，使研究人员能够在有限可观测性、不同移动模式和异质群体动态等多种条件下对奖励函数进行压力测试。我们评估了五种不同的奖励设计方案（从稀疏生存奖励到新颖的势场方法），并在多种强化学习算法（PPO、SAC、A2C）上进行了测试。通过系统性消融研究，我们发现方向性引导和明确的依从性激励是稳健策略学习的关键组成部分。我们在不同感染率、网格大小、可视性约束和移动模式下的综合评估表明，奖励函数的选择显著影响智能体行为与生存结果。使用我们势场奖励训练的智能体始终表现出更优性能，既能学习最大程度遵守非药物干预措施，又能发展出复杂的空间规避策略。该平台的模块化设计支持系统性探索奖励与行为的关系，弥补了此类模型中奖励工程研究不足的知识空白。ContagionRL是研究疫情背景下适应性行为响应的有效平台，并凸显了奖励设计、信息结构和环境可预测性在学习中的重要性。代码已开源：https://github.com/redradman/ContagionRL

Motivated by the need to systematically study how reward function design influences learned survival strategies in epidemic simulations, this paper introduces ContagionRL, a Gymnasium-compatible reinforcement learning platform. The method integrates a spatial SIRS+D epidemiological model with configurable environmental parameters to stress-test reward functions under varied conditions like limited observability and heterogeneous dynamics. The main experimental results, from evaluating five reward designs across algorithms including PPO and SAC, show that directional guidance and explicit adherence incentives are critical for robust learning, with agents trained using a novel potential field reward consistently achieving superior performance by maximizing adherence to interventions and developing sophisticated spatial avoidance strategies.
本研究旨在系统探究奖励函数设计如何影响流行病模拟中的学习生存策略，为此提出了ContagionRL这一与Gymnasium兼容的强化学习平台。该方法整合了空间SIRS+D流行病学模型与可配置的环境参数，用于在有限观测性、异质群体动态等多种条件下对奖励函数进行压力测试。主要实验结果通过对PPO、SAC等算法评估五种奖励设计表明，方向性引导和明确的依从激励是稳健策略学习的关键；使用新型势场奖励训练的智能体持续表现出最优性能，能最大程度遵守非药物干预措施并发展出复杂的空间规避策略。
Self Paced Gaussian Contextual Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Mohsen Sahraei Ardakani, Rui Song
First: 2026-03-24T22:28:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T22:28:34+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 10 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Curriculum learning improves reinforcement learning (RL) efficiency by sequencing tasks from simple to complex. However, many self-paced curriculum methods rely on computationally expensive inner-loop optimizations, limiting their scalability in high-dimensional context spaces. In this paper, we propose Self-Paced Gaussian Curriculum Learning (SPGL), a novel approach that avoids costly numerical procedures by leveraging a closed-form update rule for Gaussian context distributions. SPGL maintains the sample efficiency and adaptability of traditional self-paced methods while substantially reducing computational overhead. We provide theoretical guarantees on convergence and validate our method across several contextual RL benchmarks, including the Point Mass, Lunar Lander, and Ball Catching environments. Experimental results show that SPGL matches or outperforms existing curriculum methods, especially in hidden context scenarios, and achieves more stable context distribution convergence. Our method offers a scalable, principled alternative for curriculum generation in challenging continuous and partially observable domains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：自步高斯上下文强化学习
课程学习通过将任务从简单到复杂排序，提升了强化学习（RL）的效率。然而，许多自步课程方法依赖于计算成本高昂的内循环优化，限制了其在高维上下文空间中的可扩展性。本文提出自步高斯课程学习（SPGL），这是一种新颖方法，通过利用高斯上下文分布的闭式更新规则，避免了昂贵的数值计算过程。SPGL在保持传统自步方法的样本效率和适应性的同时，显著降低了计算开销。我们提供了收敛性的理论保证，并在多个上下文RL基准测试（包括点质量、月球着陆器和接球环境）中验证了该方法。实验结果表明，SPGL匹配或优于现有课程方法，尤其在隐藏上下文场景中，并实现了更稳定的上下文分布收敛。该方法为具有挑战性的连续和部分可观测领域中的课程生成提供了一种可扩展、有理论依据的替代方案。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the computational inefficiency of existing self-paced curriculum learning methods in reinforcement learning, which often require expensive inner-loop optimizations, particularly in high-dimensional context spaces. It introduces Self-Paced Gaussian Curriculum Learning (SPGL), a novel method that uses a closed-form update rule for Gaussian context distributions to avoid costly numerical procedures, thereby maintaining sample efficiency and adaptability while significantly reducing computational overhead. Experimental validation across benchmarks like Point Mass, Lunar Lander, and Ball Catching demonstrates that SPGL matches or outperforms existing curriculum methods, especially in hidden context scenarios, and achieves more stable context distribution convergence, offering a scalable and principled alternative for continuous and partially observable domains.
本文针对强化学习中现有自定进度课程学习方法计算效率低的问题，这些方法通常需要昂贵的内循环优化，尤其在高维上下文空间中。它提出了自定进度高斯课程学习（SPGL），这是一种新颖的方法，利用高斯上下文分布的闭式更新规则来避免昂贵的数值过程，从而在保持样本效率和适应性的同时显著降低计算开销。在Point Mass、Lunar Lander和Ball Catching等基准测试中的实验验证表明，SPGL匹配或优于现有课程方法，特别是在隐藏上下文场景中，并实现了更稳定的上下文分布收敛，为连续和部分可观测领域提供了一种可扩展且原理性的替代方案。
Operator-Theoretic Foundations and Policy Gradient Methods for General MDPs with Unbounded Costs
Authors: Abhishek Gupta, Aditya Mahajan
First: 2026-03-18T16:01:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T21:52:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Markov decision processes (MDPs) is viewed as an optimization of an objective function over certain linear operators over general function spaces. A new existence result is established for the existence of optimal policies in general MDPs, which differs from the existence result derived previously in the literature. Using the well-established perturbation theory of linear operators, policy difference lemma is established for general MDPs and the Gauteaux derivative of the objective function as a function of the policy operator is derived. By upper bounding the policy difference via the theory of integral probability metric, a new majorization-minimization type policy gradient algorithm for general MDPs is derived. This leads to generalization of many well-known algorithms in reinforcement learning to cases with general state and action spaces. Further, by taking the integral probability metric as maximum mean discrepancy, a low-complexity policy gradient algorithm is derived for finite MDPs. The new algorithm, called MM-RKHS, appears to be superior to PPO algorithm due to low computational complexity, low sample complexity, and faster convergence.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一般马尔可夫决策过程无界成本的算子理论基础与策略梯度方法
马尔可夫决策过程（MDPs）被视作在一般函数空间上对特定线性算子的目标函数优化。本文针对一般MDPs建立了新的最优策略存在性结果，与文献中已有结论存在差异。基于成熟的线性算子摄动理论，推导了一般MDPs的策略差分引理，并得到目标函数作为策略算子的Gauteaux导数。通过积分概率度量理论对策略差异进行上界估计，提出了一种适用于一般MDPs的新型主控最小化策略梯度算法，从而将强化学习中诸多经典算法推广至具有一般状态与动作空间的场景。进一步地，通过将积分概率度量取为最大均值差异，为有限MDPs设计出低复杂度策略梯度算法MM-RKHS。该算法凭借较低的计算复杂度、样本复杂度及更快的收敛速度，表现出优于PPO算法的性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the need for robust theoretical foundations and efficient algorithms for Markov decision processes (MDPs) with unbounded costs and general state-action spaces. The method employs operator-theoretic analysis, using perturbation theory of linear operators to establish a policy difference lemma and derive the Gâteaux derivative of the objective function, then integrates integral probability metrics to bound policy differences and develop a majorization-minimization policy gradient algorithm. Experimental results demonstrate that the derived algorithm, particularly the MM-RKHS variant for finite MDPs, offers lower computational and sample complexity, faster convergence, and superior performance compared to existing methods like PPO.
本文针对具有无界成本和一般状态-动作空间的马尔可夫决策过程，旨在建立坚实的理论基础并开发高效算法。方法上采用算子理论分析，利用线性算子的扰动理论建立了策略差异引理并推导了目标函数的Gâteaux导数，进而结合积分概率度量来约束策略差异，提出了一种基于最大化-最小化的策略梯度算法。实验结果表明，所推导的算法，特别是针对有限MDP的MM-RKHS变体，相比PPO等方法具有更低的计算和样本复杂度、更快的收敛速度以及更优的性能表现。
BXRL: Behavior-Explainable Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ram Rachum, Yotam Amitai, Yonatan Nakar, Reuth Mirsky, Cameron Allen
First: 2026-03-24T21:48:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T21:48:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A major challenge of Reinforcement Learning is that agents often learn undesired behaviors that seem to defy the reward structure they were given. Explainable Reinforcement Learning (XRL) methods can answer queries such as "explain this specific action", "explain this specific trajectory", and "explain the entire policy". However, XRL lacks a formal definition for behavior as a pattern of actions across many episodes. We provide such a definition, and use it to enable a new query: "Explain this behavior". We present Behavior-Explainable Reinforcement Learning (BXRL), a new problem formulation that treats behaviors as first-class objects. BXRL defines a behavior measure as any function $m : Π\to \mathbb{R}$, allowing users to precisely express the pattern of actions that they find interesting and measure how strongly the policy exhibits it. We define contrastive behaviors that reduce the question "why does the agent prefer $a$ to $a'$?" to "why is $m(π)$ high?" which can be explored with differentiation. We do not implement an explainability method; we instead analyze three existing methods and propose how they could be adapted to explain behavior. We present a port of the HighwayEnv driving environment to JAX, which provides an interface for defining, measuring, and differentiating behaviors with respect to the model parameters.
中文标题/摘要
标题：BXRL：行为可解释的强化学习
强化学习面临的一个主要挑战是，智能体常会习得看似违背给定奖励结构的非预期行为。可解释强化学习方法能够回答诸如“解释这一具体行动”、“解释这一具体轨迹”及“解释整个策略”等查询。然而，现有方法缺乏对行为作为跨多轮次行动模式的正式定义。我们提出了这样的定义，并借此支持一种新查询：“解释这一行为”。我们提出行为可解释强化学习这一新问题框架，将行为视为一等对象。BXRL将行为度量定义为任意函数$m : Π\to \mathbb{R}$，使用户能精确表达感兴趣的行动模式，并度量策略展现该模式的强度。我们定义了对比行为，将“为何智能体偏好$a$而非$a'$？”简化为“为何$m(π)$值较高？”，该问题可通过微分方法探究。我们未实现新的可解释性方法，而是分析了三种现有方法，并提出如何调整它们以解释行为。我们展示了将HighwayEnv驾驶环境移植至JAX的案例，该移植提供了通过模型参数定义、度量和微分行为的接口。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses a gap in Explainable Reinforcement Learning (XRL), which lacks a formal definition for agent behaviors as patterns of actions across multiple episodes. To enable queries like 'explain this behavior,' the authors introduce Behavior-Explainable Reinforcement Learning (BXRL), a formulation that treats behaviors as first-class objects via a behavior measure function, allowing precise expression and measurement of action patterns. They define contrastive behaviors to reframe action preference questions into differentiable queries about behavior measures. While not implementing a new explainability method, the work analyzes three existing methods for adaptation and presents a JAX-based port of the HighwayEnv driving environment to facilitate behavior definition, measurement, and differentiation with respect to model parameters.
本文针对可解释强化学习（XRL）中缺乏对跨多回合动作模式（即行为）的正式定义这一不足，旨在支持“解释此行为”的查询。作者提出了行为可解释强化学习（BXRL），通过行为度量函数将行为视为一等对象，从而精确表达和测量动作模式。他们定义了对比行为，将代理对动作的偏好问题转化为可微分的关于行为度量的查询。尽管未实现新的可解释性方法，但该研究分析了三种现有方法并提出其适配方案，同时提供了一个基于JAX的HighwayEnv驾驶环境端口，以支持行为定义、测量及相对于模型参数的微分操作。
Symmetry-Guided Memory Augmentation for Efficient Locomotion Learning
Authors: Kaixi Bao, Chenhao Li, Yarden As, Andreas Krause, Marco Hutter
First: 2025-02-03T17:00:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T21:29:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Training reinforcement learning (RL) policies for legged locomotion often requires extensive environment interactions, which are costly and time-consuming. We propose Symmetry-Guided Memory Augmentation (SGMA), a framework that improves training efficiency by combining structured experience augmentation with memory-based context inference. Our method leverages robot and task symmetries to generate additional, physically consistent training experiences without requiring extra interactions. To avoid the pitfalls of naive augmentation, we extend these transformations to the policy's memory states, enabling the agent to retain task-relevant context and adapt its behavior accordingly. We evaluate the approach on quadruped and humanoid robots in simulation, as well as on a real quadruped platform. Across diverse locomotion tasks involving joint failures and payload variations, our method achieves efficient policy training while maintaining robust performance, demonstrating a practical route toward data-efficient RL for legged robots.
中文标题/摘要
标题：对称性引导的记忆增强用于高效运动学习
为足式运动训练强化学习策略通常需要大量环境交互，成本高昂且耗时。我们提出对称性引导记忆增强框架，通过结合结构化经验增强与基于记忆的上下文推断来提升训练效率。该方法利用机器人与任务的对称性生成额外物理一致的训练经验，无需额外交互。为避免简单增强的缺陷，我们将这些变换扩展至策略的记忆状态，使智能体能够保留任务相关上下文并相应调整行为。我们在仿真四足与仿人机器人以及真实四足平台上评估该方法。在涉及关节故障与负载变化的多样化运动任务中，本方法在保持鲁棒性能的同时实现了高效策略训练，为足式机器人数据高效强化学习提供了实用路径。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the high sample inefficiency in training reinforcement learning policies for legged locomotion by introducing Symmetry-Guided Memory Augmentation (SGMA), a framework that leverages robot and task symmetries to generate physically consistent training experiences without additional environment interactions. The method extends these symmetry transformations to the policy's memory states, allowing the agent to maintain task-relevant context and adapt behavior, thereby avoiding the pitfalls of naive data augmentation. Experimental results in simulation with quadruped and humanoid robots, and on a real quadruped platform, show that SGMA achieves efficient policy training across diverse locomotion tasks involving joint failures and payload variations while maintaining robust performance, offering a practical approach to data-efficient RL for legged robots.
本文针对足式机器人强化学习策略训练中样本效率低的问题，提出了对称性引导记忆增强框架，利用机器人和任务的对称性生成物理一致的训练经验，无需额外环境交互。该方法将对称变换扩展到策略的记忆状态，使智能体能保持任务相关上下文并调整行为，从而避免简单数据增强的缺陷。在四足和双足机器人仿真以及真实四足平台上的实验结果表明，该框架在涉及关节故障和负载变化的多种运动任务中实现了高效策略训练，同时保持鲁棒性能，为足式机器人的数据高效强化学习提供了实用途径。
Dual-Gated Epistemic Time-Dilation: Autonomous Compute Modulation in Asynchronous MARL
Authors: Igor Jankowski
First: 2026-03-24T21:19:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T21:19:06+00:00
Comments: 14 pages, 5 figures. Code available at: https://github.com/xaiqo/edtmappo. Related materials available on Zenodo: 10.5281/zenodo.19206838
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
While Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) algorithms achieve unprecedented successes across complex continuous domains, their standard deployment strictly adheres to a synchronous operational paradigm. Under this paradigm, agents are universally forced to execute deep neural network inferences at every micro-frame, regardless of immediate necessity. This dense throughput acts as a fundamental barrier to physical deployment on edge-devices where thermal and metabolic budgets are highly constrained. We propose Epistemic Time-Dilation MAPPO (ETD-MAPPO), augmented with a Dual-Gated Epistemic Trigger. Instead of depending on rigid frame-skipping (macro-actions), agents autonomously modulate their execution frequency by interpreting aleatoric uncertainty (via Shannon entropy of their policy) and epistemic uncertainty (via state-value divergence in a Twin-Critic architecture). To format this, we structure the environment as a Semi-Markov Decision Process (SMDP) and build the SMDP-Aligned Asynchronous Gradient Masking Critic to ensure proper credit assignment. Empirical findings demonstrate massive improvements (> 60% relative baseline acquisition leaps) over current temporal models. By assessing LBF, MPE, and the 115-dimensional state space of Google Research Football (GRF), ETD correctly prevented premature policy collapse. Remarkably, this unconstrained approach leads to emergent Temporal Role Specialization, reducing computational overhead by a statistically dominant 73.6% entirely during off-ball execution without deteriorating centralized task dominance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：双门控认知时间膨胀：异步多智能体强化学习中的自主计算调制
尽管多智能体强化学习（MARL）算法在复杂连续领域取得前所未有的成功，但其标准部署严格遵循同步操作范式。该范式强制所有智能体在每个微帧执行深度神经网络推理，无论即时需求如何。这种密集吞吐量严重阻碍了在热力学与代谢预算高度受限的边缘设备上的物理部署。我们提出认知时间膨胀MAPPO（ETD-MAPPO），通过双门控认知触发器增强。智能体不再依赖刚性跳帧（宏动作），而是通过解析偶然不确定性（基于策略的香农熵）与认知不确定性（基于双评论家架构的状态价值分歧）自主调制执行频率。为此，我们将环境构建为半马尔可夫决策过程（SMDP），并建立SMDP对齐的异步梯度掩码评论家以确保正确的信用分配。实证研究表明，相比现有时序模型获得显著提升（相对基线获取跃升>60%）。通过在LBF、MPE及谷歌研究足球（GRF）的115维状态空间中进行评估，ETD有效避免了策略过早崩溃。值得注意的是，这种无约束方法催生了新兴的时序角色专业化，在无球执行阶段完全实现统计主导的73.6%计算开销降低，且未削弱集中式任务主导性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the inefficiency of synchronous execution in Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL), which forces agents to compute at every time step, hindering deployment on resource-constrained edge devices. The authors propose ETD-MAPPO, a method where agents autonomously adjust their execution frequency using a dual-gated trigger based on aleatoric and epistemic uncertainty, modeled within a Semi-Markov Decision Process (SMDP) framework with a specialized critic for credit assignment. Experimental results on benchmarks like LBF, MPE, and Google Research Football show the approach prevents policy collapse, achieves over 60% performance gains relative to baselines, and reduces computational overhead by 73.6% through emergent temporal role specialization, all while maintaining task dominance.
本文针对多智能体强化学习（MARL）中同步执行的低效性问题展开研究，该问题迫使智能体在每个时间步都进行计算，阻碍了在资源受限的边缘设备上的部署。作者提出了ETD-MAPPO方法，其中智能体通过基于认知不确定性和偶然不确定性的双门控触发器自主调整执行频率，该方法在半马尔可夫决策过程（SMDP）框架内建模，并采用专门的评论家进行信用分配。在LBF、MPE和Google Research Football等基准测试上的实验结果表明，该方法能防止策略崩溃，相对于基线性能提升超过60%，并通过涌现的时间角色专业化将计算开销降低73.6%，同时保持任务主导性。
